At the same time, the black giant that was under Gianni's control also tilted its right hand. Then, the armor, spear, and the clump of black ashes slid down from its palm and fell to the ground.

Seeing this, Campbell clenched his fist and bit his lip. He struggled so hard to complete his awakening, but now he was again on the verge of being killed without finding anything about the truth from the past.

Thump! Thump! The black giant started walking, and its eyes were once again filled with the deadly red lights. At the same time, Gianni spoke in Sanskrit, "As I said earlier, it would have been less troublesome for you if you just killed yourself. Now, it's too late for that. Since you wait for me to act, I won't let you die so easily. Well, I can't totally eliminate you, but I can change your will. That way, the possibility of your awakening will be reduced, and you shall live in pain for eternity!"

Just when the black giant walked past the armor and the spear, the pile of ashes scattered on the ground began to move slowly.

The scattered ashes seemed like thousands of ants that gathered bit by bit.

Then, in no time, they formed into a small pyramid, which was about ten inches high.

On the surface of the pyramid, bright red blood slowly gushed out.

The blood emitted a strange and powerful aura. As the aura quickly spread, everyone's attention was attracted to it.

"What on earth is that?" Campbell looked at the red blood on the pyramid of ashes behind the black giant. His eyes were filled with confusion as he tried to discern what it really was.

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, the Eternal Realm Hunters, and the men in black robes all stared blankly at the blood that grew out from the ashes. It was slowly taking a form of a plant's root, extending upward little by little. As it gradually formed, it almost looked like a blood coral in the sea.

"What the hell?"

Gianni walked forward and stopped at the edge of the Pure Sky Platform.

He also started staring at the transforming blood that caught everyone's attention.

Then, he immediately felt a familiar aura coming from it.

'The ancestry-level bloodline?' he thought to himself.

Before Zen entered the Three Purities Stage, he got a hold of the ancestrylevel bloodline. It dwelled in his body and gave him powerful, and sometimes, odd abilities.

Gianni was also familiar with the power of the ancestry-level bloodline, but he didn't know what ability this was.

Why was there a tremendous amount of aura from it? Gianni thought all about it and became more confused.

'What is this growing blood-red coral? Don't tell me—' Before Gianni could finish his thoughts, the blood-red coral sort of sped up its transformation.

It continued to grow until finally forming a human-shaped coral.

As the human-shaped coral stood on top of the pyramid of ashes, it suddenly started absorbing all of the ashes beneath it.

At the same time, the human-shaped coral also reached out and grabbed both the silver armor and the long spear on the ground. The armor quickly clung to the surface of its body and it held the long spear in its hand.

Finally, the cubic stone wrapped with cracks returned to its hand, and the Light of Annihilation began to flow in its hand.

Buzz! Buzz! In an instant, the armor and spear restored their silver luster.

"What is this kind of monster?" Gianni couldn't believe what he was seeing.

"He already turned into ashes, but he could still return to his original shape…"

"Is this Zen's ability?"

Everyone was in a daze as if seeing a miracle unfolding in their eyes again.

During the battle at the Pear Hill, everyone clearly witnessed the prowess of Zen's ability. He could change into almost anything and suppress even the most powerful enemies.

But even so, no one expected this time that he would just rise from the ashes as if nothing happened.

They knew how powerful he was, but they still couldn't figure out how his ability worked.

Everyone who was witnessing Zen's surprising ability was even more shocked.

That included Campbell, who was still filled with disbelief.

Those who had been baptized by the ancestry-level bloodline were known to be very powerful.

Even being turned into ashes wouldn't kill Zen.

Gianni was gazing at the scene through the black giant for a long time now, but he still didn't understand what was going on.

He didn't know that the blood that transformed into the human-shaped coral was the ancestry-level bloodline itself.

He grew pissed at the thought that Zen completely withstood his strength and power.

"I don't know what you have experienced in the Eternal Divine Courtyard.

Honestly, with such a unique ability, you're qualified to join the Ten Directions House. Unfortunately, you were not born at the right time!"

Gianni lashed out as he slapped the ground with his hand.

Then, the black giant did the same and slapped the human-shaped coral on the ground.

Buzz! Buzz! The deadly red light burst out from the black giant's palm and enveloped the human-shaped coral.

In the distance, the Snake Goddess took a deep breath and focused her eyes at the palm of the giant without blinking.

Then, the red light gradually dissipated. At the same time, the humanshaped coral also disappeared on the ground.

Soon after, everyone noticed that red corals were flickering on the surface of the black giant's arm. It was like they formed several meridians extending from its wrist up to its shoulder.

In addition to the red corals, there were also white bolts of lightning that flashed from time to time. It turned out that these were the Light of Annihilation.

Immediately after, the red and white lights intertwined and spread along its entire arm. In just a flash, its humongous arm collapsed.

Because Gianni was directly linked with the black giant, he instantly felt the pain in his right arm with the collapse of the giant's arm. "Aaargh! What did he do?!" He let out a painful scream as his face contorted.

Meanwhile, the red and white lights continued their assault and drilled into the body of the black giant this time. Gianni quickly held his chest as he felt like there was a piping hot iron stirring up his internal organs.

Buzz! Buzz! Buzz! With the power of the red and white lights, the giant's body collapsed and disappeared too.

Finally, they aimed and drilled into its head.

"No, no, no!"

Gianni clearly saw what the lights were after this time. He screamed furiously as he started feeling a sharp and piercing sensation in his skull.

Unfortunately for Gianni, he couldn't just undo his link with the black giant.

It was purposely made in complexity, so it would take time to break it.

With that, he had no choice but to endure the severe pain brought by the red and white lights.

Chapter 4025 Another Accident Gianni's wail echoed for a few seconds. At last, the black giant had finally collapsed.

Its huge body completely disappeared, and a human-shaped coral slowly descended from midair. When it reached the ground, its armor and spear fell off with a loud clatter.

Everyone stared at the human-shaped coral uneasily.

Could this be Zen? Not long after, strands of tissue and muscle started to grow on the humanshaped coral.

They intertwined with each other to form muscles and bones, and then layers of flesh rapidly formed, till finally the human-shaped coral transformed back into Zen.

When she realized it was indeed Zen, the Snake Goddess sighed in relief.

Just now, she had been so nervous that she didn't realize she was holding her breath. Now, she could rest easy.

The three Eternal Realm Hunters' jaws dropped in shock. They could not understand what was going on.

They had seen many unique and magical creatures in their time, but they had never encountered such a powerful creature with such a strange form.

Campbell was the first to step forward.

Back then, on the Whining Road, he had instinctively chosen Zen's physical body because he had a feeling that Zen was stronger than the people around him.

After awakening, Campbell knew he made the right choice. After all, Zen was a talent who could be chosen to enter the Eternal Divine Courtyard.

However, even now Campbell kept discovering that he constantly underestimated Zen.

Zen's bloodline power must've been far stronger than he ever imagined.

"Your ability comes from the life quadrant of the ancestry-level bloodline, right? Such a powerful recovery ability may be the combination of several abilities in the life quadrant. You might even be a general of the Ten Directions House!" Campbell exclaimed excitedly.

In his eyes, the generals of the Ten Directions House were invincible.

And it was true. No matter what trouble the world builders encountered, as long as the Ten Directions House sent their generals out, there was no problem that couldn't be solved.

This was also the reason why Campbell was so respectful to Gianni.

"The life quadrant?" Zen thought for a moment. "Maybe..."

When he was enveloped in the red light, he felt the ancestry-level bloodline surging within him.

The ancestry-level bloodline was not under Zen's control. At the beginning, it analyzed the information contained in the fluctuation and passed it to him.

When he came into contact with any energy, the ancestry-level bloodline would also analyze it and then gave him the energy to restrain it.

However, over time, the ancestry-level bloodline started to become cold to him. Now, if it wasn't a fatal threat, it wouldn't offer any help.

Just now, Zen fought the black giant head on because he wanted to activate the ancestry-level bloodline.

Campbell didn't ask Zen more questions about his bloodline. He turned around and looked at the other Pure Sky Platform. "But what on earth has General Gianni gone through? Why has he become so violent? Why is he so intent on throwing me back to the Whining Road?"

"The situation must be more complicated than you think," Zen said with a shrug.

On the Pure Sky Platform in the distance, Gianni was freed from the extreme pain, and his face darkened.

Campbell had awakened by accident, which was why Gianni rushed over.

However, that wasn't the only accident that happened. A lowly human had managed to kill a resentment-level Treacherous Being! How inconceivable! The Human Spirit Sect and the Ten Directions House always welcomed extraordinary talents, which was also the foundation for their growth.

However, some human spirits, like Gianni, looked down upon the human beings from the secondary worlds. In their eyes, although these human beings had inherited their looks and were very close to them in many aspects, they were still inferior.

And yet, that human was able to not only kill a resentment-level Treacherous Being, but also was reborn unharmed! How did he do it? What magic did he use? A mass of black material floated up from the Pure Sky Platform where Zen and his companions were.

It was a remaining part of the black giant.

Then, the black material changed shape in accordance with Gianni's hand movements. Soon, it formed the shape of Gianni's head.

The head was about the same size as an ordinary head, and the aura of Treacherous Being contained within it was very weak.

The space of the Three Purities Stage was very special. Both energies and materials would disappear after they left the Pure Sky Platforms. Sounds worked similarly. Thus, this was the only way Gianni could use to transmit his voice.

"How many light pillars have you triggered in the Eternal Divine Courtyard? Which light pillars are they?" Gianni asked.

The ancestry-level bloodline had three hundred and seventy-three abilities, and they could combine with each other to create many other abilities. The Four Spirits Sect had studied the ancestry-level bloodline for such a long time, but they were still unable to completely figure out its abilities.

The ability that Zen had displayed was very powerful, so Gianni wanted to figure it out.

"Sorry, I can't tell you that," Zen replied bluntly.

Gianni's expression hardened. "Aren't you afraid of death?"

"Maybe," Zen replied honestly.

Gianni's expression softened at his words. "You are of great value to us. I can spare your life, but you have to kill everyone else."

Hearing this, Campbell raised his eyebrows indignantly.

The others couldn't understand what Gianni was saying, but seeing Campbell's expression made them nervous.

Zen restrained his temper. With a smile, he asked, "Us? Who do you refer to? The Ten Directions House? Or the Human Spirit Sect?"

"You don't need to know too much. Just do as I say," Gianni said dismissively.

"Sorry, I'm not interested." With that, Zen summoned the long spear in his hand and pointed it at Gianni's head.

"Wait, wait!" Gianni said hurriedly. He didn't expect Zen would suddenly turn hostile.

However, Zen didn't give him a chance to finish his words.

The Light of Annihilation had pierced through the floating head and it burst into a cloud of smoke.

The long spear then flashed and pointed straight at the opposite Pure Sky Platform. Zen smiled faintly.

What he was interested in was Gianni's background. Since Gianni didn't want to tell him, there was no need for them to keep talking.

Gianni's eyes were filled with rage. He never thought Zen would attack him like that. This made him feel like he'd been fooled, and it was a lowly human who was fooling him! "Contact the people of the Joy House and ask them to help!" Gianni ordered in a low voice.

A brown shadow appeared beside him. It was a kind of Treacherous Being that could transmit messages.

The surface of the Treacherous Being flashed for a while, and then it said, "Master Gianni, the people of the Joy House said they can't help right now.

The Treasure Bottle Platform is being attacked."

"How dare they attack the Treasure Bottle Platform?" Gianni shouted indignantly.

"Even the Black House has rushed there, as the Joy House asked for help,"

said the Treacherous Being. "They are determined. They all want to obtain the energy that was extracted."

Gianni's expression darkened.

Chapter 4026 Treasure Bottle Platform The Treasure Bottle Platform was also a Pure Sky Platform. At the center of this Pure Sky Platform, there was a treasure bottle as tall as a person, and this was how the platform had earned its name.

One of the Godly Ways extracted from the Ways-blending Energy had been sealed up in the treasure bottle. Its purpose was to make sure no complete Ways-blending Energy was ever loosed in the chaos.

Although the chance of completing the Ways-blending Energy was not significant, the feat was not impossible.

Should someone master the complete Ways-blending Energy, it would release terrible consequences, hence, the Treasure Bottle Platform was heavily guarded, and it was virtually impossible for anyone to break in.

More importantly, the secret key in the Myriad Pagoda Mountains was well-protected. It was in the possession of a few Treacherous Beings who had awakened, and it hadn't been discovered for more than one thousand chaotic eras. How had it then come to the knowledge of someone now? Gianni sensed something unusual was afoot.

By comparison, the world builder opposite him was insignificant...

"You are lucky, but you will not be allowed to leave!" Gianni coldly said as he looked at Zen. Then he turned around and walked to the center of the Pure Sky Platform where he disappeared in the sudden flash of an orange light.

Of course, Zen and the others witnessed Gianni's departure.

"I'm afraid Gianni won't let this go," said Campbell worriedly.

Zen nodded and said, "Let's leave here for now."

At this moment, everyone's attention was once again locked on that door.

According to Campbell, the door had been replaced without anyone noticing. This door prevented anyone who entered the Pure Sky Platform from escaping it. There would be no easy escape as it was unbreakable.

"Let's work together and try again. No matter what, this door is merely an object, a dead thing. I won't believe that we can't open it with our combined efforts!" Fuxi suggested.

Previously, the situation had been dire, and everyone had tried to use brute force to open the door, but they had failed. Now that they had taken some time to consider it, everyone present was somewhat more optimistic.

"Everyone, let's use this." Thurston suddenly took out a small paper bag.

After opening the paper bag, a small block of hardened oil appeared, which wafted with a strange fragrance.

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and the others didn't recognize it, but Eastern Emperor Taiyi's eyes lit up. "Is this Dragon Beast Oil? It's such a large block!"

"Yes." Thurston nodded.

The Dragon Beast was known to be a creature that lived in the Divine River. Once it was killed, one could strip off its skin, open its stomach, and source this kind of oil there. Applying this rare oil to one's hands would greatly increase their strength.

The Dragon Beast Oil was considered a rarity in the Flaming Maple Forest.

After all, it wouldn't trigger any attack from the Flaming Maple Forest, and it could greatly increase one's own power.

This Dragon Beast Oil was therefore a treasure Thurston had cherished.

However, now in order to escape, he had no choice but make use of it.

Everyone stretched out their hands, and Thurston applied the oily substance to them.

Even Campbell, who was in the form of a Treacherous Being, applied some of it.

Once Zen applied the oil to his hands, he felt warm. Then he felt strength flow through his hands. The oil had a magical effect.

Once everyone had applied the oil, the leader of the men in black robes summoned a small golden statue with a human face and the body of a beast.

There were four round balls on its back, but three of them had been crushed. The leader said, "This treasure can double everyone's strength, but it has already been used three times. There is only one more opportunity remaining."

So saying, he reached out and crushed the last ball. With a crackling noise, two rays of golden light shot forth from the eyes of the golden statue.

As everyone stood in the halo of the golden light, they immediately felt the strength in their bodies rapidly increase! Being able to increase the power of all the warriors within the golden light by double, the golden statue was naturally no ordinary object. However, it was a pity that it would now be useless since it was used up.

In addition to these two treasures, the others also revealed their own treasures.

The Other Shore Tokens in the Three Purities Stage were naturally not ordinary. For a moment, auras of all kinds of energy circulated about in front of the door.

When they were in a state of readiness, everyone began to pull at the door! Facing the dragging of a terrifying force, the seemingly ordinary door began to tremble slightly.

"Come on, everyone. The door can't withstand much longer." Fuxi's eyes lit up.

As everyone's strength rapidly multiplied, the door shook more and more violently, as if it was about to collapse.

However, in the moment everyone anticipated the door's fall, a Sanskrit word suddenly appeared on the surface of it, and around the Sanskrit word there were intricate patterns that extended all the way to the edge of the door.

"Does this word mean 'seal'?" the Snake Goddess mused aloud as she looked in wonder at it.

The Wing King nodded. "Yes, it does."

Everyone present more or less knew some Sanskrit words, and they could even decipher some of the more complicated Sanskrit words. With this Sanskrit word being very simple, they easily got the meaning at a glance.

However, they only understood this word, but they were clueless as to the patterns on the door.

Campbell said to Zen, "It can't be opened. This is a sealed door, and it can't be broken by brute force alone."

"No matter the strength of power that is exerted on it, it can't be opened?"

Zen asked in disbelief.

Campbell nodded. "Yes, no physical power can open it."

Once Campbell spoke, no one relaxed at all. They had forced out almost every drop of their strength, but the door simply stabilized after the word "seal" appeared.

After Zen conveyed Campbell's message to everyone, the Eternal Realm Hunters and the men in black robes immediately became discouraged. The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and the other Eternal Realm warriors also gave up on trying to force the door open.

"It's such a pity that my Dragon Beast Oil has been wasted," Thurston said regretfully.

The leader of the black robed men merely shrugged his shoulders. It was obvious his golden statue was even more precious.

"What can we do now? If we can't open the door, we will be trapped here, won't we?" King Ieuan asked.

"Master Campbell, is there no other way to leave here?" Zen asked.

Studying the door for a long time, Campbell suddenly said, "Our last option is to destroy this Pure Sky Platform..."

"Destroy the Pure Sky Platform?" Zen repeated, aghast.

"Don't forget what I can do," said Campbell confidently.

Campbell's strength might be limited when it came to physical combat, but he was a world builder. All of the chaos had been constructed by him, so he understood the mysteries and principles within the chaos.

Previously, the only reason why Campbell hadn't destroyed the Pure Sky Platform was because he cared for the other world builders.

The other one hundred and ninety-nine builders in the Whining Road suffered the same malady as Campbell. Only once they returned here could they wake up.

But now, in order to leave, he had to sacrifice those considerations.

Facing the door, he swung about. Then he walked ten steps backwards, pointed at his feet and instructed, "Break open here."

Following Campbell's instruction, Zen wielded the long spear and stabbed where Campbell had pointed.

The ground of the Pure Sky Platform should have been impenetrable as the earlier fighting had done no damage to it.

"Crack!"

Unexpectedly, as Zen smashed the ground with the sharpened end of his spear, the ground cracked, revealing a rune buried within the soil.

Without so much as a glance at it, Campbell took another ten steps to the side and ordered, "Smash here."

Chapter 4027 Unfold Zen followed and smashed down per Campbell's instructions.

Crack! This last smash was strong enough and revealed a unique rune below.

Similar to the first rune, the second faced a different direction. They must be related to one another.

However, Campbell left out an explanation. He continued to walk in another direction, pointing at different areas on the ground, which signaled Zen to smash them open.

Crack, crack, crack, crack...

Zen had created more than twenty holes in the huge Pure Sky Platform. In each hole, they found a different rune.

When Zen formed the last hole, Campbell lightly pressed the rune inside. A ray of faint yellow light reflected out in response to Campbell's touch.

All of a sudden, the runes in the other holes lit up one after another. Once they were all glowing with yellow light, the ground trembled.

Bang! A muffled sound echoed from the inside of the Pure Sky Platform as if something had just opened within it.

Just then, the Pure Sky Platform slowly rotated. The stone pillars that held the armors rose one by one. At the same time, a noticeable crack appeared right at the center of the Pure Sky Platform that revealed the inside of the platform. Within the shell-like structure were patterns and complex structures.

"The Pure Sky Platform is so ingenious," Fuxi praised.

"Just like the mechanical devices below the Myriad Pagoda Mountains."

The Snake Goddess nodded in appreciation and then looked at Campbell.

"These things were probably crafted by the world builders."

"Whatever! I'm more interested in the armors! Squeak!" King Ieuan squealed, mesmerized by the display of armors within the stone pillars.

The first time they saw the armors and weapons, their interest was immediately piqued.

However, Campbell warned that the armors and weapons were protected by powerful restrictions. Afterward, they lost interest and focused on the Treacherous Beings.

Now that the entire Pure Sky Platform had unfolded, King Ieuan grew interested to obtain the armors and weapons.

"Zen, can we take some armors and weapons with us? Squeak!" asked King Ieuan excitedly.

If they utilized these weapons, they could also rely on the Light of Annihilation to get rid of the Treacherous Beings once and for all.

After pausing to think, Zen responded, "Master Campbell, these are useless if they remain here. May my friends have some? It would surely be an advantage and added protection if we go against the Treacherous Beings again."

As long as they could make use of the Light of Annihilation, everyone could defend themselves against the Treacherous Beings.

Hearing Zen's request, Campbell turned around and looked at him intently.

Though the two were at an understanding, Campbell still doubted if he and Zen were on the same side. This could also be due to his confusion with his future. As a builder of the world, he was originally a member of the Human Spirit Sect.

Having no idea what happened to his sect and why the Ten Directions House attacked him, he was full of anxiety and fear. This led him to question Zen and everyone around him, too.

At this point, Campbell was confused and troubled for a very long time.

"Do you still doubt our intention and background?" Zen asked as he noticed Campbell's sudden sadness.

"Yes," Campbell replied with a sigh.

Zen nodded. "I also do not know where you stand, but do not fear. Though you are confused now, we can help you find the truth. We will cooperate with you before we are sure of your standpoint."

Seeing the sincerity in Zen's expression, Campbell nodded in agreement.

"You know, it doesn't matter whether I take a standpoint or not. If the Four Spirits Sect was really destroyed as you said, world builders like me have no place in the world. We are useless, hopeless, and abandoned."

It took Campbell more than a thousand chaotic eras to wake up. Since then, he'd grown weary and depressed.

"You belittle yourself." Zen shook his head. "If you are truly forgotten, the Ten Directions House wouldn't have sent people here, and Gianni wouldn't have rushed over!"

Zen's words comforted Campbell. "The armors and weapons cannot be given to anyone. The other world builders need these items when they wake."

The world builders journeyed far to the Pure Sky Platform to fulfill their wishes. As much as the others wanted them, the weapons and armors were necessary for awakening. They were not for Campbell to give away.

"Not to worry. The armors and weapons are not the sources of the Light of Annihilation," said Campbell as he pointed towards the bottom of the stone pillar. "That is where important things lie. Please, take them out."

Puzzled, Zen walked towards the stone pillar and reached out his hand to feel for the bottom of the pillar.

He pulled out a palm-sized cubic stone from below, which had a grain of white sand embedded at the center. Zen brought it back to Campbell and held it out. "What's this?"

"This is a Holy Stone, but a small one," Campbell said with a smile. "The Light of Annihilation in the armors and weapons comes from this grit-like Holy Stone."

Zen was unaware of this before, and his jaw dropped at Campbell's last line.

A Holy Stone the size of a grit could provide loads of Light of Annihilation.

As he recalled, the Holy Stone snatched away from Les was a hundred times larger; no wonder the Light of Annihilation constantly flowed from it.

"The Light of Annihilation in these Holy Stones is replenished after it is used up. This is a powerful weapon against the Treacherous Beings, and everyone here can take one for themselves," Campbell said as he gestured towards the pillars.

After Zen told everyone what Campbell had said, their eyes widened in excitement, especially the three Eternal Realm Hunters.

The Light of Annihilation restrained Treacherous Beings better than any other method. No doubt it was a good weapon for the warriors to have.

With Campbell's permission, each of the others carefully took out a stone from the bottom of the stone pillar.

Once Campbell imparted the method of activating the Light of Annihilation to all of them, they put their stones away for safekeeping.

Afterward, Campbell observed the center of the Pure Sky Platform and spotted a wall beside the unfolded area. "It's time to leave here. Just need to break the wall."

Within a second, Zen flew forward and threw a heavy punch at the center of the wall.

Boom! The wall immediately collapsed with a bang and revealed a small passageway. It was so short that the ceiling of the tunnel was the height of their hips.

Zen bent down and drilled into the passageway. They all moved forward, but at around two hundred feet, they were met with another wall. Zen did not hesitate and threw another punch.

Boom! Once the wall collapsed, they were met with a large, luxurious pool.

They exited the passage one after another. When they saw the pool and the bronze statues again, they all took a breath of relief.

After the battle, the Eternal Realm warriors and the Eternal Realm Hunters did not suffer much loss. They were quite lucky to have done so.

However, more than half of the black-robed men were killed.

These men in black robes had a grudge against their leader. They risked their lives to follow Zen but inherited no benefits. Besides, many of them ended up being injured or dead for no reason.

However, the leader of the black-robed men comforted them, which allowed them to calm down eventually.

With the help of Zen, they had obtained the six-headed eagles' eggs, which meant that they saved the entire Night Being race. Because of this, they were indebted to Zen.

Moreover, they all obtained a piece of Holy Stone that they treated like a treasure. If they were faced with the Treacherous Beings again, they were prepared this time.

Chapter 4028 Reinforcement At the edge of the Freezing Wilderness, there were two crystal-like ice frogs sleeping more than a hundred feet deep underground.

This certain species of ice frogs was very rare. As long as there was no external factor that would awaken them, they could continuously sleep for about a thousand years.

Thus, they were considered as one of the most popular Other Shore Tokens that could be found in the Supreme Pure Realm.

Crack! Suddenly, a powerful force was digging from above. The huge vibration caused by it awakened the ice frogs.

Whoosh! A white mist was released from their bodies. This mist was of extremely low temperature. It could not only form a protective layer on their bodies, but also freeze the surrounding enemies to death.

However, the digger from above, who was a fire spirit from the Element Spirit race, didn't have a hint of fear for the deadly white mist.

As the white mist surged up the hole that he was digging, the fire spirit just let out a mocking laugh. In an instant, his blazing flames dispersed all of the white mist.

Whoosh! Whoosh! The ravaging flames from the fire spirit poured into the pit and mercilessly melted the ice frogs and their protective barriers.

"Hmm. They're not here. Maybe I'll continue digging westward," the fire spirit informed.

The snow that had been piled up for countess years near the snow line to the east of the Freezing Wilderness had completely disappeared, thanks to the fire spirit. It now revealed a layer of frozen black earth, which was also dug open.

The members of the Element Spirit race continued to dig deeper.

At the same time, Claire floated in the air and was overseeing the digging process. "Can't you find them in such a large area?"

The Holy Wings Armor that was floating beside Claire was actually controlled by Gavyn. He then looked into the black ground and asked, "Is it possible that they entered the Wilderness of No Return?"

Hearing Gavyn's question, Claire narrowed her eyes and there was a hint of caution on her face.

It was true that the snow line had been erased before she arrived. Thus, she thought there was a possibility that Gavyn was correct.

"It makes sense, but were they that stupid to really do it? They couldn't come back if they entered that place. Weren't they afraid of death?" Claire was still suspicious of the suggestion.

"We don't know that yet. There's a possibility that they can find a special road in the Wilderness of No Return," Gavyn speculated. "I can at least give it a try."

With that, he gently raised his hand and a door formed by blue lights immediately appeared above the palm of the Holy Wings Armor.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Several fist-sized fire spirits were released from the Holy Wings Armor.

Upon closer inspection, these fire spirits were still in their childhood.

Since their intelligence was not high enough, they couldn't decide for themselves yet and they would just follow orders.

Upon seeing that Gavyn was about to send several young fire spirits into the Wilderness of No Return, Claire lashed at him, "What do you think you're doing? Do you have to sacrifice that large number of fire spirits?"

"What are you so mad about? It's so easy to produce them. You could give birth to millions of these spirits in the Holy Wings Armor.

What's there to lose?" Gavyn sneered as he shrugged his shoulders. The Holy Wings Armor immediately made the sound of metal rubbing against each other.

"You bastard..." Claire's face darkened. She couldn't utter another word upon hearing his reasoning. She began to regret helping Gavyn take control of the Holy Wings Armor.

It was true that Claire could produce millions of fire spirits. However, in her eyes, no matter how weak the fire spirits were, they were still members of the Element Spirit race. They weren't mere tools.

But Gavyn's perspective was different. In his mind, these young fire spirits were just a bunch of flames that couldn't think on their own. And he could use them however he wanted to attain his goal.

At Gavyn's order, the fire spirits crowded against one another. They excitedly gathered and formed a huge flame.

As the huge flame reached the edge of the snow line, it quickly rushed into the Wilderness of No Return.

Swoosh! Phew! Phew! Phew! Gavyn's plan was simple and straightforward. If they found the road that they were looking for, they could return, but if not, they would die.

With that, the first fire spirit rushed into the Wilderness of No Return without hesitation.

It kept running forward until it exhausted all of its energy. Eventually, its flame was extinguished.

One by one, fire spirits continuously jumped out of the huge flame and rushed into the Wilderness of No Return.

From afar, it could be seen that there was a slanted flame line spreading forward, which looked very shocking.

"Those humans destroyed the snow line. If they entered from a particular part of the snow line, we will definitely find that road," Gavyn said confidently.

Claire also knew that this method would work. However, she was against it knowing that several fire spirits would needlessly die.

Whoosh! More and more fire spirits rushed into the Wilderness of No Return. Gavyn felt that they were getting closer and closer to the road that they were looking for.

Soon the fire spirits had reached a point that was just ten miles away from the road.

Then, there were just five miles to go.

Three miles to go.

When they were only about a mile from that road, it seemed that there was no fire spirit left to rush into the Wilderness of No Return.

"Wow, they were all used up. Release some more!" At Gavyn's command, the Holy Wings Armor opened a door formed by blue lights once more.

This time, a mass of bright blue thunder spirits had come out. These spirits continuously crackled and also began to gather to form a huge source of a thunderbolt.

There was no stopping Gavyn. The Holy Wings Armor was under his control, so he would use every member of the Element Spirit race if needed, just to fulfill his goal.

Just when Gavyn was about to give the order to the thunder spirits, a familiar voice suddenly sounded in his and Claire's minds.

"Claire, Slade, you need to come back," the Eye Spirit said.

Hearing the message, both of their expressions became serious.

If the Eye Spirit was summoning them urgently, it only meant that there was a serious situation going on.

"What happened?" Claire asked straightforwardly.

"The Nihility race is attacking the Treasure Bottle Platform," the Eye Spirit answered briefly.

She was greatly shocked at what she heard. "Those bastards, how dare they?!" she yelled in anger.

On the surface, the Element Spirit Civilization was battling against the Nihility race on the Other Shore. But the truth was, there were two more powerful forces behind them.

The Treasure Bottle Platform had always been heavily guarded by the Element Spirit Civilization. But in fact, the powerful Treacherous Beings were also there. Since the Nihility race dared to make a move, they must be pretty confident.

"Come back right now. We need reinforcements," the Eye Spirit ordered.

Naturally, it was an urgent command that couldn't be disobeyed.

So, Gavyn raised his hand and ordered the thunder spirits to return to the Holy Wings Armor.

Claire also informed the other members of the Element Spirit race that were looking for Zen and his companions in the Freezing Wilderness. After all of the members had gathered and returned to the Holy Wings Armor, an authoritative voice sounded. "Hand over the control of the Holy Wings Armor, Gavyn."

The search for Zen and the others was just a special case. Since all the elders of the Element Spirit race had left, Gavyn was tasked to control the Holy Wings Armor.

But now that all the members of the Element Spirit race had returned and merged into Slade again, they had to ask Gavyn to hand over the control of the Holy Wings Armor.

"It's not necessary right now. Didn't you hear that the matter was urgent?"

Gavyn replied.

He was actually yearning to control the Holy Wings Armor for a long time now, so he wouldn't just give it back so easily.

The collective consciousness inside Slade answered, "Yes, the matter's urgent. That's why you need to obey the order. Claire, do you think—"

Gavyn let out a cold snort, and Slade's voice suddenly stopped.

The internal world of the Holy Wings Armor was now controlled by Gavyn, so it was just easy for him to block their voices.

"I said it was not the time for that. Let's go!"

Whoosh! Gavyn spread out the wings of the Holy Wings Armor and quickly flew forward.

Claire soared in the sky and looked at the back of the Holy Wings Armor.

She kind of knew what Gavyn was thinking. Her eyes narrowed as she flew closely behind.

Chapter 4029 Giants In The River Zen and his group returned to the pool and started to crawl along the long fishing rods.

When they reached the end of the rods, they then clasped the hooks with their fingers, swinging themselves down.

In the lead were Zen, Campbell, and Fuxi. Soon after, they returned to the cave.

The moment they stepped inside, they were stunned to find a huge pile of green crystals that filled the entire cave.

The abundance of crystals completely blocked the way in.

"What the hell is that?!" King Ieuan exclaimed in its surprise.

Taking a step forward, Fuxi gently tapped on them. Examining them cautiously, he commented, "This stuff is so dense. I'm afraid it won't be easy to break—"

Before he could finish the statement, the Snake Goddess interrupted him.

"These crystals must be the Regal Jades from the Wing King's body. He was the last one to head up, so this must have been arranged by him to cover our rear."

"I think so," Zen agreed with a smile.

While the Wing King never mentioned it to him outright, Zen was rather familiar with these Regal Jades.

Once the black-robed men and the Eternal Realm Hunters followed suit and swung down, the Wing King was the last to return.

For the most part, he remained silent, bringing up the rear.

Walking to the pile of Regal Jades, he stretched out his wings and flapped at them. With that, the solid green crystals quickly melted like wax before fire and flowed toward the Wing King's body.

It wasn't long before he absorbed them all. Once he did, he stepped aside, remaining silent as usual.

In the past, the Regal Jade Civilization suffered a miserable failure when they developed a festering feud with the Nihility race. Ever since they encountered Zen in the Dark Region of Stage Thirteen, the Wing King favored Zen's superior talent, entrusting the hope of the entire Regal Jade Civilization to him.

And never had he regretted the choice, not even now. Zen had never disappointed him — instead, he greatly exceeded each and every expectation the Wing King had for him. Naturally, the latter was willing to devote himself to the man.

Once they left the cave, they returned along the path of the Wilderness of No Return.

The cave's exit stood close to the Divine River, only about thirty feet away.

Previously, Eastern Emperor Taiyi had been rather confident that this path would intersect with the Divine River. If they managed to enter it, he would have liked to dig into the soil for treasures.

Unfortunately, the cave leading to the Jade Pure Realm was the end of the path. Eventually, he had to relinquish the idea of entering the Divine River.

The minute they stepped out of the cave, the strange sight in the river had them all astonished.

Normally, the water in the Divine River was a dark-green color — the color of the Soul Interdicting Water which was preventive against Other Shore warriors from leaving the Other Shore.

The water's color never changed, save for when shoals of Golden Bites swam across the river, their bright scales illuminating the water with a golden shine.

But now, the water was dark red, emitting a strong smell of blood that spread across the river.

"How did the Divine River end up like this?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi, who happened to be the most interested in the Divine River, muttered to himself.

"It's the smell of blood," said the Snake Goddess, taking a whiff of the air.

"I don't know whose blood it is but it seems to have been flowing in the river for a long time. It's beginning to decay…"

Apart from the smell of blood, another rotten odor was coming from the river.

"Have you ever seen the Divine River like this?" Zen asked.

Both the leader of the black-robed men and the Eternal Realm Hunters shook their heads vigorously.

The Eternal Realm Hunters were rather knowledgeable, having been around the Divine River for a long time. But even they were stumped — they had never seen it like this.

"A battle happened at the upper reaches of the river," Campbell suddenly remarked.

Only Zen could understand his language, but as soon as he opened his mouth, everyone tuned in attentively. They knew he was a world builder, after all — nobody in the entire chaos could know more about it than him.

"Do the upper reaches refer to the main Pure Sky Platform?" Zen asked.

Earlier, Campbell had told him that the main Pure Sky Platform was the real Jade Pure Realm. In the end, he surmised that the upper reaches of the Divine River indeed lay in the Jade Pure Realm.

To his surprise, Campbell shook his head. "That's not necessarily the case.

When we planned the Divine River's basin, we led its water from the main Pure Sky Platform to some other smaller ones which made it meander several times…"

"The smaller Pure Sky Platforms? But they're not connected to each other.

How could they become the Divine River's basin?" Zen asked in confusion.

"We used a special method, of course," Campbell said proudly. Once he got onto the subject of his major, there was no holding him back. "It's a permanent combination of different spaces. It's only in this way that we managed to put the completed Divine River into them..."

As Campbell continued introducing the mechanism, Thurston suddenly pointed to the distance and shouted, "Look there! Something is flowing along the Divine River!"

Immediately, everyone turned to where he was pointing. An enormous figure was floating on the surface of the blood-red Divine River — it was flowing rapidly toward them.

When it got closer, they finally got a clear look.

It was a giant's corpse, lying on his side in the water.

The giant seemed to have been ruthlessly skinned — one half of him soaked in the water while the other half floated on the surface.

Half of his exposed face was swollen from all the soaking, one of his eyes wide open with anger — he seemed to have died a highly resentful death.

On the giant's dead body hopped a flock of crows, pecking at his rotten flesh.

Each of the crows only had a single eye. Despite their small size, they exuded an indescribably evil aura — it was somewhat akin to the Treacherous Beings' aura, but not quite the same.

Soon, the one-eyed crows noticed Zen and the others on the shore.

As it turned out, the crows looked more interested in fresh prey than a rotten corpse.

With a loud caw… One of the crows took the lead and flew away from the Divine River, heading straight for Zen's group.

But just as it reached about ten feet, an invisible force suddenly wrapped around its body, dragging it forward against its will. Failing to return to the river, it went straight into the depths of the Wilderness of No Return.

The same thing happened to the rest of the crows. Once they left the range of the Divine River, all of them were affected by the mysterious power, reluctantly flying toward opposite directions.

Everyone heaved a sigh of relief at the sight. Their nerves had been going wild because the one-eyed crows seemed to be highly powerful creatures of the Jade Pure Realm. Nobody knew what abilities they possessed nor did they have any idea how difficult it would be to deal with them.

When Zen asked Campbell if he knew of these Other Shore creatures, the latter only shook his head in reply.

While it was true that he was a world builder, he already left to find the next suitable spot once the previous world was completed. Because of this, he knew little of the later developments in the secondary worlds. Without having experienced much of the chaos' development, he could only offer so much information.

For a while longer, they lingered on the bank of the Divine River.

In a short period of time, they witnessed six more dead giants flowing down along the river. With that, they concluded that the river must have turned red because of the great amount of blood from the giants.

Whoever had killed them, though, remained an enigma to them.

After taking the time to observe the area, they returned along the same path they had come. Encountering no obstacles in the wilderness, they found the journey back was rather smooth.

But when they arrived at the snowline, much to their surprise, they found an area of bare brown earth.

Chapter 4030 Divide Into Two Groups Eastern Emperor Taiyi gazed around him, frowning. "If memory serves me right, this should be a thick snow field," he muttered.

The field was brown and completely devoid of any snow.

All the ground within a radius of several miles was sunken to a depth of over a hundred feet.

It seemed clear what had happened. The Element Spirit Civilization had dug far and wide into the depths of this former snow field.

The Snake Goddess shrugged, looking unperturbed. She said, "The Shadow Marks can last for five days. Although the Shadow Warriors didn't monitor us directly, it wouldn't have been difficult to find this place using the marks."

After entering that road in the Wilderness of No Return, the Snake Goddess had used her shadow to destroy the snow line.

In hindsight, it seemed to have been a wise decision. Otherwise, they would be blocked halfway by the Element Spirit Civilization.

They carefully observed their surroundings, keeping a sharp lookout for anyone from the Element Spirit Civilization. After they had ensured that they were alone, they crossed the snow line and returned to the Freezing Wilderness.

Immediately, the body of the Wing King began to expand. His humanshaped figure transformed into the form of a giant hawk, with a wingspan at least several hundred feet wide. He spread his wings and the group of people clambered onto his back, whereupon he soared into the open sky above the Freezing Wilderness.

When they were about a third of the way across the Freezing Wilderness, the leader of the black-robed men turned to Zen. He bid him goodbye and thanked him one last time.

Previously, he had decided to follow Zen as far as he could in order to repay him. Moreover, although their race had always lived in the Dark Region, they had a great relationship with humans.

While they had been able to offer some help during the fray, the leader was very clear that the true strength of the Night Being race could only be displayed in the Dark Region. Once they reached the Light Region, it would be difficult for them to fight against enemies. Indeed, they would only be a burden.

Before leaving, the leader gave Zen a piece of black silk. He explained that it was a way for Zen to call upon them for assistance—should the silk be torn anywhere in the Dark Region, the Night Being race would instantly know his location. Zen acknowledged the gesture, and the black-robed man left with his remaining clansmen.

After they departed, the Wing King spread his wings and rose once more over the vast Freezing Wilderness.

Occasionally, they caught sight of a few creatures in the snow below them.

The creatures watched and pointed at the group flying in the sky, their faces filled with malice, as though they would attack them if given the chance.

However, the Wing King flew too swiftly for anyone to catch them. Before they could take action, he had turned into a green light and escaped far away.

Campbell stared out across the vast expanse of white snow. His eyes were hooded, but there was a glimmer of sadness in them. He had always wanted to awaken, but unexpectedly, he had been abandoned after awakening. For a long while he was silent as they flew. Then suddenly, he leaned closer to Zen and asked, "Can you tell me about what happened in the past? Can you tell me what history you know over the past thousand chaotic eras?"

Zen did not look surprised at the sudden questions. He nodded and gave Campbell an overview of the chaos history he was familiar with. Of course, there was some sensitive information that he kept to himself.

Campbell listened closely. When Zen was done, he asked, "So the two strongest forces in the chaos are the Element Spirit Civilization and the Nihility race?"

"Exactly," Zen replied, nodding.

"Yet they are only puppets, controlled by unknown forces with their own ulterior motives," Campbell remarked disapprovingly.

Zen raised an eyebrow, considering Campbell's statement. He said, "I think so too."

Zen himself had not realized this before entering the Supreme Pure Realm.

As he got to know the Treacherous Beings and met Gianni of the Ten Directions House, he had learned more about the Element Spirit Civilization and the Nihility race. In reality, their backgrounds were quite complicated, and a far cry from the simple history he had imagined.

"You are all alone with no reinforcements. It's really surprising that you have come this far," Campbell observed, turning his head to look at the Eternal Realm warriors on the back of the Wing King.

Although Campbell had not been very strong back then, he was clear about the strength of this group of Eternal Realm warriors. It was impossible for them to fight against the forces behind the Element Spirit Civilization and the Nihility race.

"That's right," Zen agreed. He decided to take the opportunity to request help from Campbell. "I hope that you can help us complete the Finale Way and prevent the chaos from being destroyed again."

The chaos had been destroyed repeatedly because the Four Spirits Sect needed to extract energy from it.

Campbell lowered his head, saying nothing. After several moments of contemplation, he said, "If you are correct that the Four Spirits Sect has been exterminated, then it is indeed meaningless to continue destroying the chaos. I can help you to figure out the truth, but I must also save my companions from the Whining Road. I need to awaken them."

"We will awaken them. I believe it can be done without any trouble," Zen said with a confident smile.

Zen and his group had gained a preliminary understanding of the Treacherous Beings from his communications with the leader of the blackrobed men on the Pure Sky Platform.

The Treacherous Beings were divided into several types in accordance with their different wishes. For instance, those on the Whining Road belonged to the attaching type. They sought to possess other living beings in order to go to the Pure Sky Platform and retrieve everything they'd had before their death. If they were successful in completing this goal, they would naturally awaken.

Thus, they only needed to send some creatures into the Whining Road and allow the Treacherous Beings to possess them. The Treacherous Beings would wake up after they went to the Pure Sky Platform to get what they wanted.

Zen turned to the Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and the others. He told them, "Master Campbell wishes to awaken his companions."

They knew Campbell was referring to the one hundred and ninety-nine Treacherous Beings on the Whining Road.

"Wake them up, you say?" said King Ieuan. It mulled over the idea.

Meanwhile, the Snake Goddess was thinking quickly, formulating a plan.

She said, "In that case, we must capture one hundred and ninety-nine creatures on the Other Shore. We will bring them into the Whining Road."

Fuxi said, "It shouldn't be difficult. Although the creatures in the Three Purities Stage are not to be trifled with, there are still some relatively weak races. As long as we have enough time, we can do it. But of course, the top priority right now is to save the heroes of the human race."

Based on the plan devised by Zen and the Primeval Lord of Heaven, they would begin to rescue the human heroes trapped in the underground after entering the Supreme Pure Realm. But they had lost time while Zen was possessed by Campbell.

It would take a long time to save the Treacherous Beings on the Whining Road now.

When Fuxi finished speaking, something began flowing from the back of the Wing King. Dark green liquid oozed out from beneath the feathers. The green substance pooled together and rose to form a body, turning into a human-shaped Regal Jade statue.

"Zen, ask if this Regal Jade statue can be used," the Wing King instructed.

Zen asked in Sanskrit, "Master Campbell, will your companions possess this Regal Jade statue?"

Campbell studied the Regal Jade statue, then nodded. His eyes brightened with satisfaction. "Yes, they will!"

In fact, the Treacherous Beings on the Whining Road didn't need to possess other creatures to awaken. The reason for possessing other creatures was their desire to use the Light of Annihilation to kill the Treacherous Beings with big heads. But now that all such Treacherous Beings had been killed, they could simply walk straight out of the Whining Road.

However, they still wanted to realize their long-cherished wishes. The Regal Jade statues made by the Wing King would lead them out of the Whining Road and enable them to reach the Pure Sky Platform.

"Well then, we can divide into two groups. I will go to the Whining Road to awaken those Treacherous Beings, and you go to open the underground passage to save the heroes of the human race," said the Wing King gravely.

The Snake Goddess nodded. "I agree. It's a good arrangement."

There was an empty thatched hut since Campbell had left the Whining Road, and it would be safe for the Wing King to enter it alone.

As soon as everyone had voiced their approval of the plan, the Wing King sent them to the Myriad Pagoda Mountains. Then he changed his route.

Wings spread, casting an enormous shadow on the ground below, the giant hawk flew alone towards the Blood Swamp.

Chapter 4031 On The Treasure Bottle Platform In the Jade Pure Realm, on the immense, hundred mile long and wide Pure Sky Platform, stood a huge treasure bottle in the shape of a gourd.

It was crystal clear and beamed magnificent colors as light reflected off it and refracted through it.

A wide river flowed beside the treasure bottle, appearing out of the void of the Jade Pure Realm and passing through the Treasure Bottle Platform.

This was the famous Divine River.

Many giants' corpses lay on either side of the Divine River.

Blood gurgled from their bodies and into the river through the drains, dying it a blood red.

A fat monk stood beside the corpses, smiling relentlessly. He appeared kind and friendly by his face, but the blood soaked into his robe said otherwise.

He grabbed a corpse and pushed it into the Divine River.

Splash! The body drifted down with the current.

On the opposite side of the river, a woman in a long robe was covered in blood as well, her once pure white robe now a deep red. Like the fat monk, she too was pushing corpses into the river.

The fat man might have looked like a monk, but he was in fact a Taoist priest. His name was Darby and he was the eldest disciple of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

The woman was Stella, the youngest of the Grandmaster of Heaven's disciples.

"I did not expect our master to kill so many giants in only three days. His strength must have increased significantly," sighed Darby.

The giants in the Jade Pure Realm possessed terrifying strength.

Facing so many was incomprehensible. If Darby came face to face with just one, he would be forced to retreat.

Being the eldest disciple, not only did he have all kinds of treasures, but the bloodline he had obtained from the Eternal Scroll Painting was extremely magical too. He was definitely among the top figures of the many Eternal Realm warriors.

A speck of worry appeared in Stella's eyes. "Our master has indeed become stronger, but did you notice that he seemed almost entirely not himself during the battle?"

"It's understandable. He was so determined to kill his opponents that perhaps he forgot himself a little and was not as kind as usual," Darby said as if this was common knowledge.

But Stella shook her head and replied, "No, it was more than that. It felt to me that he was possessed by a Treacherous Being.

Do you remember how our sister died?"

Darby darkened at the mention of their sister and scolded, "Don't ever mention her again!"

The sister they were talking about was the second disciple of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

She took care of Samantha, Sienna and Stella like a mother and they treated her as one.

The Grandmaster of Heaven once encountered a powerful enemy and in the heat of battle, he lost control. He bullied his opponent back, forcing him to retreat before he slaughtered him like a mad man.

Although he was victorious, in his wildness, he had accidentally killed his second disciple.

This shadow of hurt had always lingered in Stella's heart. It was a difficult reality for all three sisters to face.

Stella had buried the matter within the depths of herself, but the way the Grandmaster of Heaven mauled his way through all the giants in a craze brought it all back.

She had been standing close to one of the giants as he rampaged. If Darby hadn't dragged her away, the Grandmaster of Heaven would have killed her as well.

When she looked into his eyes, an uncontrollable shiver ran through her. As she looked at him, he was not a person anymore, but a disgusting Treacherous Being.

They had won the battle on the Treasure Bottle Platform, but the thought of the look on her master's face unearthed memories of her big sister and made her terribly uneasy.

She hadn't expected such a harsh reaction from Darby when she mentioned their dead sister.

But Darby's heart softened when he saw the grief on her face and immediately made an attempt to comfort her. "Master has his worries too.

Many things are not as simple as they seem. How do we fight the Element Spirit Civilization? Do you think it's possible for Master to do this alone?"

As the outside world saw it, the Grandmaster of Heaven alone led the Nihility race in the fight against the Element Spirit Civilization. However, very few knew the truth and even Stella and her other two sisters were clueless as to it.

Stella pursed her lips and calmed down, admitting in a low voice, "I know.

No matter what kind of person he is, he will always be my master."

Splash! Darby pushed another giant's corpse into the Divine River and the water rippled as it fell. With a smile, he said, "That's right. We shouldn't doubt our master."

Many of the elites of the Nihility race were from other races, but only nine, including the Grandmaster of Heaven, were humans. Naturally, they had always been close with one another.

Four red spheres floated under the massive treasure bottle.

Powerhouses of different shapes floated in these red spheres. They all advocated the Nihility Way and some were leaders of their races on the Other Shore.

With their faith in the Nihility Way, they did all they could to destroy absolutely everything, and so it made sense for them to follow the Grandmaster of Heaven.

They were Ewing, Sloan, Phelps and Larson.

They each used their own theurgies in an attempt to open the treasure bottle.

But all their efforts were in vain as the bottle remained motionless. On the bottle was a single Sanskrit word, "seal", and around the word were thick lines that extended all over the bottle.

They knew the sturdiness and stubbornness of the bottle were related to the word on it, but none of them could find a way to break it.

"What on earth is in the bottle that the Element Spirit Civilization has to protect it like this?" Ewing's rough voice asked from one of the red spheres.

"In addition to the numerous giants, there are also so many hostility-level Treacherous Beings. Whatever is in this bottle must be very valuable,"

Phelps speculated.

"I didn't expect us to not be able to open the bottle after we took the Treasure Bottle Platform. This is really embarrassing."

As the four were deep in discussion, the Grandmaster of Heaven sauntered over.

He wore a golden robe that fluttered even though there was no wind. He was a truly intimidating figure to behold.

Swish! He stretched out a hand and drew a black dagger from his waist. It was not made of gold, copper or jade, but instead looked like the tooth of some kind of monster.

"That's the tooth of someone in the darkness! How did you get that?" Sloan, who looked like a cat and was the first on the left, asked.

The Grandmaster of Heaven didn't answer him. He leaped gracefully and nailed the black dagger firmly in the Sanskrit word, and the lines strewn across the bottle began glowing as he did.

The light faded and the lines that had been used to sustain the bottle turned into cracks.

A pale yellow energy emitted from the bottle, shocking the four powerful creatures when they saw it.

"Huh. The aura of this energy is awfully weak."

"Apparently, this is the aura of the Godly Way. But is it really a Godly Way?"

"Indeed, the aura is extremely unusual. Upon closer inspection, it doesn't belong to any of the three thousand Godly Ways. However, it does look like the aura of the Godly Way."

And even if their cultivation of a Godly Way actually reached the peak level, they would merely acquire one divine megaton of force. Why on earth would they be interested in it? At any rate, they had been staying in the Supreme Pure Realm for such a long period of time. This meant that they weren't aware of the news circulating in the Grand Plain Stage.

In addition to that, the Grandmaster of Heaven had never divulged any information regarding the Evil God.

"I assure you, this is indeed the Godly Way energy," the Grandmaster of Heaven stated frankly. He didn't want to beat around the bush.

The four red spheres were rotating simultaneously. When they heard the Grandmaster of Heaven's confirmation, they exchanged meaningful glances.

They paid a great price in order to capture the Treasure Bottle Platform.

Despite that, all they got was the Godly Way energy. They couldn't accept that this was it.

They had a hard time wrapping their heads around it. Was the Grandmaster of Heaven insane? They all thought so. Why else would he choose to grab this? Nevertheless, the Grandmaster of Heaven always had the most accurate predictions. He even managed to help them escape from death countless times. Obviously, he would never do such a boring thing.

"So what's the use of the Godly Way energy anyway?" Phelps decided to go along with the Grandmaster of Heaven's train of thought. He might as well learn what his purpose was.

"You are from the Other Shore. Therefore, you have never set foot in the chaos before. Ewing, go ahead and tell him what the use of the Godly Way energy is," instructed the Grandmaster of Heaven.

While Phelps was from the Other Shore, Ewing, on the other hand, was from a ruling civilization that existed in the chaos.

When the Grandmaster of Heaven called his name, Ewing had an inscrutable expression on his face. "The Godly Way energy helps one reach the consummation of True God Realm and subsequently break through to the Other Shore Realm," he answered.

When Phelps, Sloan, and Larson heard his answer, they merely broke into laughter.

The Other Shore Realm was quite insignificant to them.

The Grandmaster of Heaven slightly turned blue in the face as he restrained himself from reprimanding them. He turned around to face Ewing and asked, "Do your race not cultivate the Ways-blending Energy?"

"Huh? The Ways-blending Energy? Why would we? Isn't it just a waste of time?" Ewing questioned. In his honest opinion, cultivating the Waysblending Energy was far inferior to entering the Other Shore. As a matter of fact, most of the Other Shore Realm warriors had the same notion even until now.

The Grandmaster of Heaven sighed and felt a bit frustrated. "The main reason why the Ways-blending Energy isn't that strong is that it has always been flawed. Remember, the six great truths are all derived from the Waysblending Energy. The complete Ways-blending Energy is actually very powerful."

Even as he tried to explain it, Phelps, Larson, and Sloan still didn't understand what he meant. After all, the three of them were from the Grand Plain Stage on the Other Shore. And there, they had almost no chance to learn about the concept of the Godly Way.

However, Ewing had a serious expression on his face. He felt like he had heard of this before.

When he was still in the chaos, he didn't cultivate the Ways-blending Energy. However, his now deceased brother was very obsessed with it. His brother had actually spent a lot of time on it. Sadly, the final result was not good.

Later on, his brother told him that the Ways-blending Energy was extremely powerful. The only drawback was it could be extremely difficult to blend the Godly Ways. More importantly, the energy was incomplete and defective.

At that time, Ewing didn't take his brother's words seriously. He simply thought that he had failed in cultivating the Ways-blending Energy, so he just used it as an excuse to save face.

What the Grandmaster of Heaven said strongly reminded him of what his brother also told him once before.

"The complete Ways-blending Energy may be extraordinarily terrifying,"

Ewing mumbled quietly. The words came out of his mouth as though from a long forgotten memory.

The Grandmaster of Heaven smiled when he heard this. "That is precisely why I wanted to attack the Treasure Bottle Platform."

As soon as he finished talking, he took out a small bottle. "Collect!" he said to the pale yellow energy floating in the air.

Swoosh! The bottle gave off such an attraction force.

The pale yellow energy floated noiselessly in the air. Trapped in the treasure bottle for many chaotic eras, it had now become intelligent. It was struggling very hard to get out of that attraction force.

However, it was too weak to resist it. Soon enough, it was sucked into the bottle.

At this very moment, everyone heard a strange sound out of the blue.

"Meow..."

The meow was very soft. It was almost like a newborn kitten's cry.

They could tell that the voice came from afar but it could be distinctly heard from all over the place.

"Is there a kitten somewhere? I heard a meow," Stella asked confusedly.

She had just thrown a giant's corpse into the Divine River. However, even the loud splash of the water was unable to cover up the meowing sound.

Darby was a lot more sensitive than Stella was. Without warning, his spiritual sense had spread out and covered the Pure Sky Platform.

Instinctively, he turned around and aimed at the northern area.

The Grandmaster of Heaven brought out a wooden cork from his waist band. There were elegant runes carved on the cork. With it, he covered the mouth of the bottle and gently tapped the runes with his fingertips.

Buzz! The runes on the cork flashed and firmly sealed the bottle.

After that, the Grandmaster of Heaven raised his head and smiled at the void. "I have a question for you."

He held the bottle firmly in his hand and shook it. The bottle had an interesting feature. It would change its color in accordance to the color of the thing inside it. Therefore, the elegant white porcelain bottle had now turned yellow.

"Now that the Godly Way energy has been successfully extracted, why should you not destroy it right away?" the Grandmaster of Heaven asked.

"Meow..."

They heard another meow echoing through the entire area.

"There may only be one truth," the Grandmaster of Heaven answered the question himself. "The energy of the entire chaos is constant. Even if you destroy this Godly Way energy, it would just be reproduced somewhere else in the chaos. Is my speculation correct?"

"Meow..."

The meow had gotten even louder and much clearer.

In an instant, they seemed to realize that it had a terrible magic power. As the sound faded away, everyone who heard it felt agonizing pain in their ears. It was almost as if they were actually getting clawed by a cat.

"Ouch! That hurts!"

Stella screamed and covered her ears with her hands.

When he saw this, Darby turned his hand upward and a small golden bell appeared on his palm.

He loved collecting treasures. He carried over a thousand of them with him all the time.

He gently tossed it upwards. In the blink of an eye, the small bell turned into a big golden bell that covered him and Stella. At the same time, it kept chiming softly, which effectively alleviated the pain in their ears.

Phelps, Larson, Ewing, and Sloan also used their own methods of protecting their ears from the shrill and piercing cries.

On the other hand, the Grandmaster of Heaven remained standing still and made no effort to cover his ears. He merely stared toward the north.

From the outside of the Treasure Bottle Platform, an enormous cat head slowly appeared. It had a white ball embedded on the top of it, which was filled with numerous eyeballs. They noticed that these were not illusory eyes, but real ones. Each and every one of them was connected by blood vessels in a very complex manner.

This being was actually the leader of the Element Spirit Civilization, the Eye Spirit.

All of a sudden, a booming voice came out of his body.

"Do you really think you can easily get away with something that is not yours?" he asked them in an intimidating manner.

"Shouldn't the Treasure Bottle Platform be a trap? It could be just like what I did to those puny humans before?"

"What do you think?"

After the Eye Spirit finished talking, Phelps, Larson, Sloan, and Ewing felt ill at ease. Meanwhile, the Grandmaster of Heaven remained as calm as usual.

Chapter 4033 Possession Of Treacherous Beings The Element Spirit Civilization had always regarded the Treasure Bottle Platform as a very important place for their race. It was heavily guarded by the Joy House.

For the longest time, the members of the Nihility race had never even considered attacking the Treasure Bottle Platform.

But this time, the Grandmaster of Heaven was able to lead them inside.

They fought their way in and killed all of the members of the Joy House.

The plan went too smoothly that it felt like a trap.

The Grandmaster of Heaven looked around then sneered. "It has taken me some time before I managed to lure out and vanquish the ghosts of the Joy House. But now, it seems like they were just baits. Does it mean that this is some sort of bait as well? Or are you freely handing it over to me?"

After saying this, the Grandmaster of Heaven faced towards the Eye Spirit and shook the pale yellow bottle in his hand.

All of a sudden, one of the Eye Spirit's eyes opened wide and fixed its stare at the bottle. It glared with such force that...

Swoosh! The Grandmaster of Heaven's arm was completely chopped off by the eye's intense stare. The severed arm still held the bottle in its hand. Both had instantly disappeared and reappeared beside the Eye Spirit.

"Grandmaster of Heaven! Your arm..." Phelps yelled in shock. He stared at it with a frown.

Ewing, Sloan, and Larson exchanged nervous glances. They couldn't believe what just happened.

However, they thought the Grandmaster of Heaven wouldn't have been so careless. Maybe he had a trick up his sleeve. Nevertheless, they were still a little worried when they saw his bloody arm.

They needed not worry because at the next moment, the arm and the bottle that appeared beside the Eye Spirit suddenly exploded. They merely turned into a mass of colorful smoke.

Seeing this, the Grandmaster of Heaven smiled and calmly took out a white silk cloth to cover his wound. Astonishingly, the broken arm had been recovered when he pulled the silk cloth off. The bottle was still in his hand.

He continued to shake the bottle towards the Eye Spirit. "It was simply magic."

All at once, each and every eyeball on the Eye Spirit's body blinked. They looked at the Grandmaster of Heaven with disgust and pure loathing.

The huge cat under the Eye Spirit got up with its back arched. Its fur stood on its ends as it started to emit an extremely foul and repulsive aura. This was a resentment-level Treacherous Being. It was known to be exceptionally powerful among its kind.

The revolting aura immediately began turning into visible black waves.

Darby's golden bell was a powerful defensive treasure. However, the surface of the bell was instantly riddled with holes as the black waves washed over it. Under the pressure of the black waves, Stella was about to collapse.

"Darby, take Stella away from here," the Grandmaster of Heaven ordered at once.

He was the Grandmaster of Heaven's eldest disciple. Therefore, he clearly knew how and why his master had suddenly become so powerful.

Whenever a battle involved Treacherous Beings, the Grandmaster of Heaven would no longer be human. He would transform into a Treacherous Being, or half human and half Treacherous Being.

There was a time when Darby also wanted to obtain such power. He thought it was a very convenient and useful ability.

Therefore, he and Maynard Zhao had made so many requests for their master to teach them.

After all, they often had to face Treacherous Beings whenever they traveled within the Three Purities Stage. It seemed reasonable that they learned how to use that power as well.

It didn't matter whether the Treacherous Beings were strong or weak. They always had no other choice but to run away from them. It was even difficult for them to move a single step when faced with these monsters.

Nonetheless, the Grandmaster of Heaven refused their requests right off the bat. In return, he gave each disciple a strange stone. The Light of Annihilation was contained within each of the stones. It could easily kill the Treacherous Beings.

All of his eight personal disciples had one.

Even though the stone was only the size of a small bean, the Light of Annihilation contained inside it could effectively slay the Treacherous Beings.

Stella, Sienna, and Samantha were the weakest among the disciples. But even they could kill the Treacherous Beings with the help of their stones.

Whoosh! After Darby and Stella gained enough distance, they noticed a lump of soil rising from the flat ground in front of them. It was like a tomb without a tablet.

When Darby saw the bump, he instantly pulled the silver curtain and released Stella from it.

The stone given by her master was embedded in her sword. In this way, she would be able to inflict serious damage to a Treacherous Being.

Stella wouldn't normally use this sword to defend against any other enemy.

But whenever she encountered a Treacherous Being, the sword would always come in handy.

Buzz! It started emitting a powerful energy.

She raised her long sword then positioned it horizontally at the level of her head. The stone embedded on the hilt was emitting the Light of Annihilation. It began covering the edges of the sword.

Meanwhile, a long stick appeared upon Darby's shoulder. His stone was embedded on the center of the stick. The Light of Annihilation emitted by the stone radiated towards both ends of the stick.

The creatures under the bump seemed to have noticed the enemies outside.

Hostility-level Treacherous Beings were relatively weak. They could easily take them out if there were just a few of them. Unfortunately, they came in a large number this time.

Squeak! Squeak! Squeak! One by one the monkeys began to move.

In the meantime, Darby's long stick released thousands of white stick shadows. It smashed the monkeys into pieces in the blink of an eye.

With their outstanding expertise, they efficiently annihilated all of the monkeys that came from the lump of soil.

After so many years of patient cultivation, Darby was almost as strong as the Grandmaster of Heaven. Therefore, Stella had complete confidence in his abilities.

Chapter 4035 Cat And Saber Generally speaking, most Eternal Realm warriors and Other Shore creatures felt apprehensive at the mention of the Treacherous Beings.

Chapter 4037 Stone Men Clang! Clang! The rocks in the cave-dwelling were smooth and solid. The sounds of the stones colliding with each other as they rolled down were especially crisp.
