Sawyer took a close look and said, "These stones seem to be the earth spirits of the Element Spirit race."

The earth spirits of the Element Spirit race could turn themselves into extremely sturdy stones. They could just be differentiated from ordinary ones because of their unique aura.

"What? Why would they turn into these?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked in confusion as he also inspected the huge pile of stones.

The Element Spirit race once trapped the human heroes in this cavedwelling, so they might have been sent here to guard the place. But still, they were confused as to why they would turn to these inanimate objects.

"Look! Something is coming out from the walls!" the Snake Goddess quickly warned as she pointed at a wall nearby.

Then, they saw masses of white orb-like things emerged from within the walls.

Judging from the form and the aura they emitted, there was no doubt that they were Treacherous Beings.

"Treacherous Beings!"

"Watch out for them!"

"Be alert! Those who could use the Light of Annihilation, be prepared for their sudden attack!"

After entering the Supreme Pure Realm, they had suffered a lot from the hands of the Treacherous Beings. Thus, they developed an instinctive vigilance whenever they faced them.

From the aura that they were releasing, it was safe to assume that they were hostility-level ones. But as for what type of Treacherous Beings they were, they still couldn't tell.

Whoosh! Whoosh! There were a total of three Treacherous Beings that emerged from the walls.

No one knew what their original form was. When they came out of the walls of the mountain, they were just like flowing water. Then suddenly, they rushed into the pile of stones.

At this moment, they didn't understand what the Treacherous Beings were trying to do. They began pulling several stones and pillars that gradually turned into three huge stone men.

As Zen and his group saw this, that was when they realized the goal of the Treacherous Beings for rushing into the stones that were actually made up of earth spirits.

"These hostility-level Treacherous Beings are vulnerable in the face of the Light of Annihilation, so the Element Spirit Civilization used the earth spirits to serve as their physical bodies," the Snake Goddess muttered.

Everyone's face immediately became serious as they faced the combined prowess of the Treacherous Beings and the Element Spirit race.

They had already experienced the terrifying power of the Treacherous Beings on the Pure Sky Platform, but they still didn't know much about them. On the other hand, the Element Spirit Civilization seemed to be pretty familiar with how the Treacherous Beings functioned, as they even made fortified bodies specially designed for them.

"What should we do now?" King Ieuan asked as it started to panic. "Well, what choice do we have? We have to kill them using the Light of Annihilation," the Snake Goddess said with a straight face.

"But with those bodies, they won't be afraid of the Light of Annihilation now, right?" King Ieuan said reluctantly.

"Then we do it in a straightforward manner. We break those stone bodies, drive out the Treacherous Beings inside, and kill them," Zen declared decisively. "Master Campbell, can you assist me?"

Campbell nodded at Zen's request.

When he left the Pure Sky Platform with them, he had also put on his silver armor and taken his long spear with him.

As a Treacherous Being himself, he would be pretty useful in battles against them.

Most importantly, if the Light of Annihilation wasn't used on him, he wouldn't be affected. Thus, he had an incomparable advantage in dealing with the Treacherous Beings that hadn't awakened yet.

Just as he took a step forward, Campbell's body suddenly froze. "Zen, it seems like they're well prepared," he said in a low voice.

The three stone men seemed to have immediately sensed Campbell's aura.

A white dot of light appeared on each of the huge round stones on their shoulders. A ray containing the Light of Annihilation was instantly produced and was about to burst out at any time.

"Damn it! The Element Spirit Civilization has calculated everything!" Fuxi shouted as he gritted his teeth.

As the dominator of the Other Shore, the Element Spirit Civilization had an unfathomable foundation. They were powerful and wise that they almost had no weakness. Now, Fuxi and the others just felt how terrifying they could be as opponents.

"Get back! Let me handle them!" Pearson stepped forward and took the initiative to attack the stone men first.

"Keep them busy and I'll find a way to break their bodies," Zen instructed Pearson as he borrowed the long Spear from Campbell. Since Campbell couldn't risk fighting the stone men, Zen had to take charge. The surface of the long spear had been specially customized so that the Light of Annihilation could easily spread to the spear's tip.

As the Light of Annihilation burst out from the Holy Stone in Zen's palm, the twelve-foot long spear emanated a dazzling silver light.

Since the Treacherous Beings had an instinctive fear of the Light of Annihilation, they instantly felt the threat oozing out from Zen's spear.

Buzz! Buzz! Then, the runes on the chests of the three stone men began to glow with red lights.

Whoosh! Whoosh! The surface of the stones transformed into thorns, stretching outward. In a flash, the stone men became huge hedgehogs made of stones.

Thud! Thud! Thud! Discerning that Zen imposed the greatest threat, they immediately rushed towards him.

Pearson let out a smile as his body began to vanish bit by bit. His entire body transformed into countless threads that sneakily lay in wait for the movements of the stone men.

As soon as they rolled toward Zen, they were instantly tripped by countless silk threads, slowing down their movements.

As Zen saw this, his body quickly flashed and appeared above the head of one of the stone men.

The Treacherous Being inside the stone man was quick to react. As it saw Zen above its head, it instantly leaped and tried to impale Zen's body into the stone thorns all over its body.

Zen instantly noticed what it was trying to do. He grabbed on one of the stone thorns and maneuvered his body to dodge its attack.

"Zen, watch out! Another one's coming from behind!" King Ieuan yelled.

Zen saw that another stone man whose body was covered all over with thorns was rushing over at great speed.

Although Pearson's silk threads had slowed down their movement, they were still fast enough to not be underestimated.

Whoosh! With Zen's fast-thinking, he grabbed the long spear and pressed its bottom part against the body of the stone man he was holding, and placed it horizontally.

Just before the stone man rushing behind made contact with him, he leaped high up. The two stone men collided harshly and the spear pointing towards the second stone man was forcefully stabbed into its body.

"Aaaargh!"

Shrilling screams came from the Treacherous Being inside the stone man's body.

The spear enveloped with the Light of Annihilation pierced cleanly into the body of the hostility-level Treacherous Being. With the power of the Light of Annihilation, it was instantly killed.

Whoosh! Zen rushed toward the body of the dead stone man and quickly pulled out the long spear. Before the other stone man that collided with the dead one could get up, he dashed over to its side.

Crack! Before it could even react, the long spear impaled into the other stone man's body. With a hissing sound, the second Treacherous Being was immediately killed.

After quickly eliminating two of the three stone men, Zen looked at the other side of the cave-dwelling.

The third one was blocked and was being taken care of by Sawyer, Thurston, and Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

At the same time, the Snake Goddess and Fuxi were waiting patiently to launch their attack. Then, suddenly, Eastern Emperor Taiyi finally drove his golden sword into the sturdy body of the last stone man, leaving an opening on the surface of its body. Fuxi immediately took action and used the opportunity to attack the Treacherous Being inside.

As he rushed towards the stone man, his palm showed a snow-white light which was actually the Light of Annihilation.

Clap! With the impact of Fuxi's palm enveloped by the Light of Annihilation, the Treacherous Being inside was instantly reduced to a pile of ashes.

Fuxi waved his hand with a hint of pride in his eyes.

Previously, during their first encounter with the Treacherous Beings, he thought that they were completely invincible.

He still clearly remembered the fear they instilled in his heart as they passed the Whining Road for the first time.

But now that he possessed the Light of Annihilation, he turned his fear into rage and determination and would kill them easily.

Chapter 4038 The Broken Passageway Once all three Treacherous Beings were killed, the stones stopped moving.

Though these stones were formed by the earth spirits, they remained as mere piles of dead things.

Zen cut the stones carefully and took out the Holy Stones within. These Holy Stones were about the size of a grain of sand.

He did not know just how many stones Element Spirit Civilization had but he considered them a rare treasure and they would be very useful if he encountered a large number of Treacherous Beings.

After he put the stones away, Zen and the others continued to venture into the depths of the cave.

The path was not complicated and all they needed to do was go down.

As they went deeper, the path got wider and there was a continuous draft that blew above their heads.

"It seems there is a hidden pool or river here in the cave," Eastern Emperor Taiyi told them.

Zen nodded at his observation. "There is indeed a pool at the end of the cave. Your real selves are trapped beside that pool."

Eastern Emperor Taiyi couldn't help but flinch when he heard the word "real'.

It wasn't long ago after he was rescued from the Divine River that he found out there was a "real" version of himself so he still wasn't that used to the concept.

Fuxi and the Snake Goddess had long since accepted the fact that they were their creators' avatars but it was going to take Eastern Emperor Taiyi a bit more time to do so.

Realizing the slip of his tongue, Zen quickly tried to correct his mistake.

"I'm sorry."

"It's fine," Eastern Emperor Taiyi assured him with a smile. "I'd actually like to see what the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi looks like!"

Not long after, a pool appeared before them.

The water was so clear that they could see the bottom of the pool.

King Ieuan looked around. "I don't see any of the human heroes..."

"How can that be? This is a dead-end. There is no other way up ahead," the Snake Goddess seconded, walking around to search for the human heroes.

Zen also circled around the pool once and released his spiritual sense in an effort to find something like a hidden passage. Unfortunately, he came up with nothing.

Ever since the Primeval Lord of Heaven told him that he didn't sense the existence of the real human heroes through the Civilization Artifact, Zen had begun to mentally prepare himself for this sort of result. It didn't hurt any less, however, when he looked around and found nothing but an empty cave.

Yasamin looked at the others with a frown. "Do you think they've already been taken away by the Element Spirit Civilization?"

"They were trapped here for quite a long time. Maybe they've already been killed," Pearson murmured.

The Eternal Realm Hunters did whatever they could to hide but in the end, only three of them managed to survive. It was truly highly unlikely that they would still be alive after so long.

"There's another possibility," the Snake Goddess said as she pointed upwards. "What if they went on to the Jade Pure Realm?"

Unlike Pearson, the Snake Goddess chose to be more optimistic. The roads in the Myriad Pagoda Mountains all led to the Pure Sky Platforms after all, and this cave was no exception.

Since the human heroes were trapped in this cave for so long then that meant they had all the time in the world to ascend to the Jade Pure Realm.

Zen nodded in agreement with this assumption. "Master Campbell, do you know how we can go to the Jade Pure Realm?"

As a world builder, Campbell was undoubtedly the one who was the most familiar and knowledgeable about all this. "I know that this path leads to the Night View Island. It's a huge and independent Pure Sky Platform.

Unfortunately, I didn't design this path. Let me think for a second..."

Though he was a world builder, Campbell only partly participated in the construction of the chaos. He didn't know about all the specifics.

Fortunately, he was quite close to his colleagues and had a general understanding of what they did when they built the passages. He walked towards the pool and scooped out a handful of clear water. Soon enough, a smile broke through his features.

"Boil the water," he told Zen.

The man's eyes widened in astonishment. "Boil the water?" he repeated to make sure he heard Campbell right.

It wouldn't be difficult since the pool wasn't that big but Zen was just caught off-guard by the strangeness of the request.

"Yes. Don't worry, you'll find out why when you boil it," Campbell assured him.

Since there was really nothing else to do, Zen took on Campbell's strange request and jumped into the pool. He originally wanted to activate the Godly Way energy but the Primeval Lord of Heaven who was in Zen's inner world was too impatient and directly asked Zhurong to move.

There was a flash of red light and the entire pool immediately began to boil.

Zhurong's powers were at work and if he went all out then he could instantly evaporate the water within the pool.

As the entire pool boiled, a miraculous scene appeared.

A crooked red path appeared in the originally clear and transparent pond.

This path exhibited many twists and turns as it extended all the way down to the bottom.

Pearson, who always had a deadpan expression, sported a look of surprise.

"Is that the entrance?"

The Snake Goddess nodded. "I think so."

Fuxi could only stare at the sight in shock. "To think the entrance is actually hidden like this. Who would ever have thought of boiling the water?"

Once upon a time, the thirty-nine human heroes got trapped here and tried every means to find the passage out of this place. At some point, one of them probably boiled the water on accident and discovered what was previously hidden.

Zen soon emerged from the water and waved everyone in to follow him as he swam along the red path.

Not willing to be left behind, everyone quickly jumped into the water and followed Zen.

It wasn't until they reached the bottom that they saw a door constructed out of pure light open for them. Zen entered first, followed closely by his companions.

"Splash!"

As soon as he crossed the threshold, Zen immediately felt as if his world was spinning. He was previously swimming downward but now everything was upside down and he was headed upwards.

When his vision stabilized, he saw a passageway above him.

They were very familiar with this passageway. They had grabbed onto fish hooks when they went to the first Pure Sky Platform, but it seemed they had to manually swim their way up this time to reach the Pure Sky Platform they were heading to.

Nobody talked much, too focused on moving their limbs to swim their way up. They'd eventually reach their destination this way, right? Wrong.

The group swam for quite a while but there was no indication that they were getting closer towards the Pure Sky Platform. Zen quickly surfaced and found himself in the middle of the passageway! Splash! Splash! Splash...

Everyone looked around in confusion when they saw where they were.

King Ieuan was the first to speak. "We're still in the passageway?"

"Look!" the Snake Goddess exclaimed as she pointed upwards.

They originally swam upwards in an effort to reach the Pure Sky Platform.

However, when they looked up, they saw that the passageway was cut in half. They were in the lower half and the other half of the passageway hung above their heads.

"This passageway seems to have been intentionally destroyed by someone,"

Eastern Emperor Taiyi remarked in observation.

"Who?" King Ieuan asked. Just who would do such a thing? "Maybe we're right and the real human heroes did arrive at the Pure Sky Platform," the Snake Goddess said as she continued to look up.

"Why do you think so?" Yasamin asked.

"If those real human heroes found this passageway then they would safely arrive at Pure Sky Platform. However, the Element Spirit Civilization would still be hot at their heels," the Snake Goddess stated with a smile. "If they truly wanted to escape then they had to make sure they couldn't be followed. Breaking the passageway was the best choice to make sure their pursuers would never be able to go the same way they did."

Chapter 4039 The Possibility Of Repair According to Campbell, this place called the Night View Island was an independent Pure Sky Platform.

There was no way to cross the Pure Sky Platforms. Once the passageway was destroyed, the pursuers could no longer chase the human heroes.

The Snake Goddess judged reasonably.

Both Zen and the Primeval Lord of Heaven in his inner world agreed.

"Since the passageway is broken, can't we fly there?" suggested Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

The passageway hanging above was reachable that everyone could easily fly to it.

"Let's have a try."

The Snake Goddess snapped her fingers and her shadow stretched out from behind her. It then turned into a blood-red bird and flew upward.

At more than one hundred feet away, the shadow disappeared without a trace. It appeared to be swallowed by a monster in the void.

The Snake Goddess narrowed her eyes, surprised. She shrugged at Zen and said, "It seems that this place also belongs to the Jade Pure Realm."

The area beyond the Pure Sky Platforms in the Jade Pure Realm devoured all the energies and materials in it. It was dangerous to fly there.

Zen looked at Campbell floating on the surface of the water and asked, "Master Campbell, can you find a way through this passageway?"

Campbell didn't answer. Instead, he swam to the edge of the water and stretched out his hand to explore outside the passageway. "We can't pass through it," he said. "There's so much Void Dust in this area."

"Void Dust?" Zen asked with a puzzled look.

Campbell replied, "The Jade Pure Realm is filled with dust that cannot be seen. You can imagine it as invisible dust, and anything that gets close to it will be devoured."

The shadow that the Snake Goddess released was indeed devoured by the Void Dust.

These people were subject to many restrictions since they were all from the chaos.

The core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization was already of great power in itself. Aside from helping Zen understand Sanskrit, it could even restore the white light dots in the Abstruse Energy World.

However, the so-called Void Dust didn't have a white light dot, so the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization was unable to decode it.

The others attempted to access the area, following the Snake Goddess's example.

Pearson released a living creature. It was a black bat from the Supreme Pure Realm which was highly toxic. Pearson wanted to tame it for his use after capturing it, but he had not succeeded. Therefore, he decided to throw it away.

Whoosh! After departing from his hand, the black bat darted forward like a weapon.

It didn't know where it was, but it was glad that it could finally get rid of Pearson. No one could catch its speed now.

However, its excitement lasted only for a short while. Coming to its senses, it felt its body being devoured and quickly disappeared.

Energies couldn't make it through the passageway, and neither could living creatures.

"There is a way to deal with the Void Dust. Only the Spiritual Boat can pass through it, so I don't know what exactly to do," said Campbell after the bat had disappeared.

Zen and the Primeval Lord of Heaven in his inner world were saddened.

The hearts of the Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and all the other heroes sank after the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization translated Campbell's words.

"So this Pure Sky Platform is a dead end?" Zen asked hopelessly.

"In a sense, yes." Campbell nodded and thought for a while. "Unless we find a way to repair the passageway."

"Repair the passageway?" Zen's eyes lit up.

Seeing the excited expression on his face, Campbell smiled as he shook his head. "Forget it. There was a way back then, but over a thousand chaotic eras have passed. I'm afraid the material needed doesn't exist anymore."

"What material?" Zen asked.

He knew that the material needed to repair the passageway was by no means ordinary, but he was unwilling to give up.

The energy souls of the Primeval Lord of Heaven and the other people in his inner world were also waiting. As long as there was the slightest chance, they refused to quit.

"It's the Eternal Twilight Seed," Campbell said. "It looks like a copper pea and it's found in the main world."

"The seed from the main world..." Zen murmured.

In his inner world, everyone's face was painted with hesitation.

When it came to the Abstruse Energy World, everything was extremely complicated. They couldn't do anything about it.

"The Eternal Twilight Seed is very unique. It is actually a kind of metal but is also a plant. It is a live metal that grows up with superior stability," said Campbell, his hand patting the edge of the passageway. "After its metal branch stretches out, the hollow branch will form a passageway and a huge, flat corolla is formed at the end. With some simple pruning, it will quickly form a Pure Sky Platform."

During that time, it was a mature plan to build the top of a world with the Eternal Twilight Seed. It was also a necessary skill for every world builder.

Zen raised his eyebrows slightly upon Campbell's mention of the metal branch. "Master Campbell, how big is the branch of the Eternal Twilight Seed?" he asked.

"It will be this huge after the seed fully grows up," said Campbell, pointing at the passageway. The passageway and even the Pure Sky Platform sprung from the Eternal Twilight Seed.

"But the branch that has just sprouted is about this big," Campbell said extending his arms.

"Is it metal-colored all over, with flower on it?" Zen's eyes glistened.

The conversation between him and Campbell relied on the group of people singing in his inner world. Naturally, Campbell and the others couldn't sense his mood fluctuations.

However, when he transmitted his words into his inner world, his voice was abnormally excited.

Even the Primeval Lord of Heaven, the Snake Goddess, and the others also experienced violent mood swings.

Campbell nodded. "That flower is the one that needs to be pruned. Have you seen one before?"

On Zen's right hand, an azure square appeared out of nowhere. He reached out his hand, gently pinched it, and took out a metal branch. "I wonder if this is the metal branch you mentioned," he said, showing it to Campbell.

Not long after Zen entered the Other Shore, he obtained this metal branch in the Sacred Mallow Temple.

He had once shown it to the Primeval Lord of Heaven and the others, but none of them knew what it was.

Campbell glanced at the metal branch and took it from Zen's hand. "At least two thousand Pure Sky Platforms hadn't been completed at that time, and these two thousand Eternal Twilight Seeds must have all sprouted and grown into such branches."

The metal branches were exquisite in appearance. They didn't respond to any energy, so they couldn't be used as Other Shore Tokens. It was believed that they had some magical characteristics yet to be discovered.

However, they couldn't grow into Pure Sky Platforms without the world builders.

In addition, normal methods couldn't destroy them. For more than a thousand chaotic eras, they had spread all over the Other Shore. Zen had encountered just one of them.

The Dreaded Eye Demons obtained a metal branch by chance. Like many other races on the Other Shore, they studied it for a long time but didn't find out how to use it. In the end, they hid it in the Sacred Mallow Temple as rubbish, only to be retrieved by Zen later.

Chapter 4040 The Lake King Ieuan stared intently at the metal branch for a while. Finally, it couldn't contain itself and blurted, "Zen, what's the use of this thing?"

Even Eastern Emperor Taiyi, the Snake Goddess, and the Eternal Realm Hunters were curious.

After all, they couldn't understand the conversation between Zen and Campbell.

"This metal branch can be used to make a Pure Sky Platform," Zen answered. "It should also be able to repair this passageway."

"Really?" Fuxi couldn't conceal the excitement in his voice.

"Every cloud has a silver lining," the Snake Goddess said with a gentle smile. She wasn't surprised that Zen's luck was taking a turn for the better.

"I once sold two such branches," King Ieuan said wistfully. "Everyone thought that they were useless. They were so hard to sell!"

Everyone glanced at King Ieuan speechlessly.

Even Zen was a little surprised, but he quickly understood why.

The metal branches had an extraordinary appearance. According to Campbell, two thousand Eternal Twilight Seeds grew into metal branches at that time, but they were not able to form Pure Sky Platforms.

These metal branches were difficult to destroy, so it wasn't unusual for them to show up on the Other Shore.

If a creature obtained one, it was inevitable that they wouldn't be able to unravel the mysteries within, so their best bet was to just sell the metal branch. It was not strange that King Ieuan came across one or two of these in the past.

What was important now was there was hope to repair the Pure Sky Platform, but first, they needed to leave the passageway.

Campbell took everyone back through the passageway. When they reached the bottom, they reached a dead end. The entrance was nowhere to be found! "Boil the water," Campbell ordered.

From Zen's inner world, Zhurong was about to make a move but then Pearson suddenly said, "Let me do it."

As he spread out his hands, blood red flames blossomed around his body.

Like magic, the entrance that had vanished now reappeared! Everyone shuffled through the entrance and stepped into the cave. The pool in the cave was connected to the passageway, so the water in the pool was also boiling.

"Zen, take your companions out of the pool," Campbell barked.

Zen nodded and took everyone to leave the pool.

Once the last person had stepped out of the pool, Campbell stood on the surface of the water, his expression becoming extremely serious.

He used to be an expert in building worlds, but he hadn't done this for many years.

Splash! He put one hand in the pool and began to stir the water gently.

Although his movements were gentle, the pool began to quake violently.

Splash! Splash! Soon, a huge whirlpool was formed inside the pool, and it spun towards the entrance at the bottom of the pool.

At the same time, Campbell raised the metal branch high above his head.

He reached out to grab the air beside the metal branch. He didn't touch it, but it suddenly began to shake.

Then, the look on his face grew more serious. He gently picked the metal branch, and then a white dot of light appeared on its bottom.

"This light dot..." Zen raised his eyebrows curiously.

Logically speaking, there shouldn't be any white light dots in the chaos.

The only exception in the chaos should be the Cold Prisons, due to the extremely low temperature.

But now, the metal branch broke this rule, which naturally surprised Zen.

As Campbell continued to pick, light dots appeared one after another. After these light dots fell into the whirlpool in the center of the pool, they were pulled into the entrance at the bottom of the whirlpool. From there, they drilled into the passageway to the Jade Pure Realm.

The others didn't understand what these dots of light entailed, but Zen did.

The core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization continuously deciphered these light dots and transmitted a picture to Zen's eyes. Then he saw that one end of the metal branch had grown rapidly and spread into the water, until finally it drilled into the bottom of the pool.

Splash! Splash! As the water in the pool whirled faster and faster, more and more parts of the branch extended into the pool.

In the others' eyes, they could only see more and more white light dots emerging.

However, the passageway in the Jade Pure Realm underwent big changes.

After the white light dots drilled into the Jade Pure Realm, they quickly formed a huge metal branch, which was still growing steadily. The metal branch quickly drilled through the broken parts of the passageway and grew all the way to the Pure Sky Platform.

Then the metal branch became thicker and thicker, gradually filling the entire passageway.

Crack! Crack! As the metal branch expanded, cracks appeared on the surface of the old passageway and chunks of it fell off, until all that was left of the broken passageway was a pile of debris.

When the broken passageway collapsed, a shiny new metal branch appeared.

There was no white light spot released from the metal branch in Campbell's hand, but the bud at the top of the metal branch was shining with a bright red light, as if it was about to bloom at any moment now.

Once the bud bloomed, it would form a huge Pure Sky Platform.

However, if the Pure Sky Platform was formed here, the people present would be crushed to death.

Campbell carefully sealed the bud up. The bright red light disappeared and was replaced with a dull grey color.

"Zen, can you give me the rest of the metal branch?" Campbell asked.

Zen smiled faintly. "It belongs to you. I'm just returning it to its rightful owner. You don't need to ask for my permission."

Campbell nodded and smiled back. After putting away the metal branch, he said, "The repair has been completed. You can go in now."

Everyone once again jumped into the water and swam into the passageway along the brand new, glowing red path in the pool.

The size and width of the passageway were exactly the same as before, but the inner wall looked very new. After all, it had just been completed.

"Creak! Why is this new passageway also full of water?" King Ieuan asked as it swam upward.

The Snake Goddess speculated, "Maybe the end of this passageway is connected to a water source. When the new passageway was formed, the water naturally flowed down quickly to fill the entire passageway."

King Ieuan was somewhat skeptical. When it swam to the end of the passageway with the crowd, it was surprised to find that they ended up in another pool of water.

When they finally reached the surface of the water, they all came out with a splash. As they took in their surroundings, their eyes widened in surprise.

It was just as the Snake Goddess said, they were in the center of a lake.

The Night View Island was a very huge Pure Sky Platform. Although it was not as big as the main one, it was over a thousand times larger than the one Zen and the others had been to before. The lake in the center of the island occupied more than half of its area.

The lake was surrounded by grayish mountains. In the night, these mountains were like demons and monsters lying on the ground, emitting a quiet and unsettling aura.

Although this place was not the main Pure Sky Platform, it was still within the Jade Pure Realm.

According to the information they had obtained so far, the Treacherous Beings should come from the Jade Pure Realm.

So it wouldn't have been surprising if they encountered powerful Treacherous Beings here in the Night View Island.

After they left the surface of the water, they flew closely to the mirror like lake. Everyone, including Campbell, tried to move as quietly as possible, so as to not draw any attention to themselves.

Chapter 4041 The Strange Pattern Zen flew ahead of the group. Just as he was about to reach the lake shore, he spread out his spiritual sense.

The spiritual sense was a handy method of surveying one's surroundings; it made studying things at a distance easier, and even the things hidden underground could be detected by it.

However, just as Zen's spiritual sense swept over the terrain beside the lake, a strange image suddenly appeared in his mind.

It was a circle with ten animal teeth hanging around it! Crack! The circle spun violently, and the animal teeth began to flash ominously.

Then, Zen suddenly felt a stabbing pain in his mind, which made him almost cry out.

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and three Eternal Realm Hunters also released their spiritual senses, as Zen did. They also saw the circular pattern. In unison, they all started crying out in pain.

"Ouch!"

"What is that? It hurts!"

"My spiritual sense is affected..."

When Zen came to his senses, he glanced back at the Snake Goddess, Fuxi and the rest in dismay.

"Do you see anything with your spiritual sense?" the Snake Goddess asked.

"A ring with ten teeth embedded in it," Pearson replied concisely.

"I saw it, too! Squeak! Squeak!" King Ieuan exclaimed with a pained expression.

Fuxi studied the bank of the lake in the distance, his forehead creasing in fear.

Under normal circumstances, one should be able to send out their spiritual sense unimpeded. However, some special things could block the spiritual sense.

There were even more powerful things and creatures that could devour the spiritual sense, causing it to disappear without a trace.

This time, their spiritual senses didn't bounce back or disappear after moving around the area. However, what their spiritual senses revealed was the ring inlaid with teeth.

This was very strange, as though someone had deliberately shown them this.

Everyone discussed in low voices, but they couldn't seem to come to a conclusion.

Zen asked Campbell about it, but even Campbell was confused. "The Night View Island is a relatively large Pure Sky Platform, and we haven't arranged anything on it," he said. "I've never heard of the ability of affecting the spiritual sense that you just mentioned..."

As the builder of the world, Campbell was very familiar with the chaos and even the worlds outside it, but even his knowledge was limited here.

"I'll go ashore first, and you follow me," suggested Zen.

The people present had witnessed Zen's almost endless life energy, so they all nodded in agreement.

Zen flew to the lakeshore quickly. He was about to land on a large boulder.

Boom! The second Zen's foot stepped on the rock, a sickeningly loud explosion went off in his ears. His forehead seemed to have been hit hard by a heavy wooden stick. The moment his mind went blank, the ring inlaid with teeth appeared again! "What happened?" Zen frowned, wincing in pain.

Although what just happened was a bit strange, Zen figured it was still safe enough to call the others. Zen still said to the Snake Goddess, "You all can come over now. Be careful when you land. There seems to be a strange spiritual attack..."

The Snake Goddess nodded and went ashore with Fuxi and the others.

Boom! As soon as the Snake Goddess landed on the ground, she was also hit heavily. Her face turned pale, but after a while, she seemed to gather her bearings.

The same thing happened to Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Yasamin and the rest.

The reactions of King Ieuan and Fuxi were the greatest. They fell on their knees, writhing in pain.

Campbell, on the other hand, landed with ease. He was the only one who didn't feel anything when he stepped on the ground.

"I saw that ring again..."

"There is no spiritual attack nearby...."

"What is this?"

Everyone was filled with worry, especially the three Eternal Realm Hunters.

They had lived in a dangerous environment for so long, and they were trained to stay vigilant at all times. If they were not careful enough, they were in danger stumbling on death's door. Usually, when they encountered this phenomenon which was hard to explain, they figured the best they could do was to keep highly vigilant and be suspicious of everything.

"Primeval Lord of Heaven, try to communicate with the Civilization Artifact again," Zen said to the Primeval Lord of Heaven in his inner world.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven had already been prepared. With Zen's order, he appeared on the top of the book. As the pages were turned, the Civilization Artifact tried to contact the real human heroes.

The energy souls of the real human heroes, including the Snake Goddess, Fuxi, Emperor Charm, Zhurong and the others, also gathered around the book. They all wanted to know the result as soon as possible.

Splash, splash...

The pages stopped moving, and it began to glow with a green light.

The energy souls of human heroes immediately connected to the book, trying to accept the information that was transmitted from the book.

Boom! The reaction of these energy souls was exactly the same as that of Zen and the others when they landed on the shore. They had also been attacked and seen the ring with ten teeth...

Although the energy souls still had their powerful theurgies, they were very weak in terms of soul. A stronger soul attack was enough to seriously injure them.

However, the ring's attack did not cause any damage. It only made the people who saw it wince in pain.

Although these energy souls covered their heads and cried for help, thankfully, they were not injured at all.

"Even the Civilization Artifact can be affected..." Zen was speechless.

"The Night View Island might be enveloped by some kind of magical power. You can only explore it with your physical bodies," the Primeval Lord of Heaven suggested.

Zen nodded. They had come a long way to get here, and it was futile for them to even consider giving up.

Although the Night View Island was by no means small, they hoped to be able to gather some clues around the ominous-looking mountains.

Surrounding the lake shore was a greyish-white forest.

When he was flying past the lake earlier, he saw that everything on the Night View Island was grey-white, and now even the forest was in the same color. Out of curiosity, he went forward and picked a leaf. As soon as he took the leaf from a tree, a layer of grey-white ashes fell to the ground, revealing a large emerald leaf.

It turned out that these trees were not grey-white, but their surfaces were covered in a layer of ashes! "Is there any volcano on the Night View Island?" The Snake Goddess's eyes narrowed.

If there were any volcanoes on this island that erupted, it would explain why the entire place was covered in ashes.

Fuxi shrugged as he reached out to pick a leaf. Cautiously, he sniffed at the dust on the leaf, and said, "This is not volcanic ash. There is no smell of sulfur."

Zen also asked for confirmation from Campbell. Campbell said that there was no volcano set up on the island when the Night View Island was built.

"There has to be some reason why there's dust all over the island..." Sawyer scratched his chin, pondering aloud.

"No." Pearson shook his head and pointed at a place not far away. "Look, the ashes are not evenly distributed. Only the flowers and trees have ashes, but there is no dust in other places..."

After careful observation, Zen and the others found that what Pearson said was true.

Except for the flowers and trees, there was no ash on the rocks and the ground.

"This is very strange," the Snake Goddess said with a deep frown. "Either the ashes belong to the plants, or they have been sprinkled on them by someone..."

Just as everyone was confused, Zen saw something from the corner of his eye. Turning to see what it was, he was surprised to see that a white claw stretched out from one of the trees with a handful of ashes, carefully sprinkling them on the leaves.

The emerald leaves Zen just dusted were now covered in grey-white ashes once more.

Chapter 4042 The Ghost Powder The white claw continued to scatter ashes.

Soon, the emerald green leaves were covered with a layer of ashes again.

Zen and the others stood still and carefully observed the movements of the claw.

Even from afar, they were sure that it was a Treacherous Being.

However, they noticed that the disgusting aura emanating from the creature was not as strong as those of the previous ones that they had faced.

Although thick leaves were blocking their view, they could still make out its appearance. It was like a sluggish sloth that actually looked adorable.

After the sloth-like Treacherous Being spread a layer of ashes on the plants, it jumped down from the branch and slowly approached Zen's group.

"What does it want to do now?" Fuxi asked as he stared at it warily.

Seeing that the Treacherous Being started walking towards them, Sawyer and Thurston instinctively took out the sand-sized Holy Stones. Just before they activated the stones, Pearson stopped them and looked at them while shaking his head.

Zen actually had the same thought in mind. He just stood still and watched the creature as it walked towards him.

As a native of the place, the creature was much more familiar with the environment than them. Moreover, the fact that it was an immortal and had low intelligence meant that there should only be few things that could scare it.

"If that's not the case, then does it want to help us instead? But I don't think that's more plausible," Yasamin said coldly as her eyes were glued to the Treacherous Being.

"Well, there are different kinds of Treacherous Beings. Some like to possess other creatures, while others like killing. "I don't know about that… These monsters are just—"

Zen hushed Yasamin before she could utter another word. He knew what everyone thought about the Treacherous Beings, but he also thought that the Snake Goddess was right. There were so few things that they knew about them, so they couldn't just conclude anything.

After the sloth-like creature repeatedly pointed at the sky, it reached into a pouch in its abdomen. It was filled with the grayish-white ashes that it had been scattering. It grabbed a handful of the ashes and attempted to sprinkle them on Zen's feet.

As a conditioned reflex, Zen immediately stepped back to avoid the ashes.

The creature sensed Zen's vigilance upon its action, so it started pointing towards the sky again. Its eyes revealed a trace of sincerity as if pleading him not to avoid the ashes. Afterward, it walked towards Zen again with some ashes in its hand.

At this moment, a feathered arrow suddenly shot out from a distance.

Whoosh! The arrow gushed at an incredible speed, and it firmly nailed the ground just in front of the creature.

At the sight of the arrow that instantly landed in front of it, the sloth-like creature was startled. It made a few somersaults and hurriedly climbed a tree.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Two arrows fired in rapid succession and shot towards the tree where the creature hid.

Even with the thick forest blocking the shooter's view, the arrows that were shot landed accurately. They struck the trunk of the tree, and the creature was directly behind it.

Swish! Swish! The sloth-like creature quickly got down from the tree and rushed deeper into the forest to hide.

Although they realized that the arrows were not aimed at them, Zen and the others didn't let their guards down.

With this, the three Eternal Realm Hunters dispersed and looked around.

Deeming that it would be much faster to call out the one responsible for it, Fuxi yelled coldly, "Who shot those arrows? Show yourself right now!"

As soon as he finished speaking, a short creature emerged from the other side of the forest. His attributes were very similar to a human child's. His face was just a bit bigger than usual, but was actually good-looking. He could just be differentiated from humans because of his long green tail with a flat leaf-like end.

"Don't be afraid. I've just driven off the Treacherous Being," the short creature said.

When everyone heard that he could speak the standard human language, their tensed bodies began to relax a little.

The Night View Island was a very anomalous place. Though they hadn't encountered any extreme danger, they might instantly fall into a bad situation if they were not careful enough in this unknown environment.

That said, it would be great if someone could be their guide.

They immediately thought that he could be a big help since he looked so kind and sincere, and he also instantly helped them drive off the Treacherous Being.

"Thank you for your help and I apologize for yelling before." Fuxi cupped his hands and showed his gratitude to the creature.

You were in grave danger just now," he continued.

The smile on Decker's face instantly vanished as he started explaining, "Every night, certain creatures will come down from the sky. They will come here and devour all the living things that are sprinkled with the Ghost Powder."

When they heard this, there was a variety of expressions that appeared on their faces.

Some frowned, while others raised their eyebrows. Some eyes widened, and some mouths opened.

Zen was one of the most shocked because his feet were almost sprinkled with the Ghost Powder. The three Eternal Realm Hunters exchanged glances with each other.

All of them were utterly shocked. No one could hide their surprise and anxiety as they heard what Decker said.

In the last Pure Sky Platform, they happened to face a resentment-level Treacherous Being. If it weren't for Zen's explosive power at the most critical moment, they would have been dead already.

It wasn't an understatement to say that they just got lucky to surpass that hurdle. They were not even sure if they could successfully beat a resentment-level Treacherous Being next time. Now, if it was true that hatred-level Treacherous Beings would come and assault them, there probably was a zero chance of them surviving.

Instinctively, King Ieuan, Yasamin, and the others took a few steps back.

They were relatively close to the part of the forest where the sloth-like creature sprinkled the Ghost Powder. Knowing that it could attract the hatred-level Treacherous Beings, they had to make sure that they had absolutely no contact with it.

"You said that the hatred-level Treacherous Beings only attack the living things that are sprinkled with the Ghost Powder. So, as long as we don't come into contact with it, we should be fine then, right?" Zen asked after thinking about it for a while.

Then, with an innocent smile on his face, Decker answered, "Hmm, no. You will still be in danger."

Chapter 4043 Collecting "You are outsiders. Of course, you don't know the cruelty of the Night View Island. Generally, outsiders are killed on the first night!" Decker's face turned pale. "The Night View Island is full of Treacherous Beings. There are a lot of hostility-level Treacherous Beings which are the weakest ones.

Although Zen tended to believe the Treacherous Being, the Treacherous Being did not have intelligence and he could not obtain information from it.

He would pay a price if he misunderstood the meaning of the words.

It can be used in critical moments!"

Swoosh...

The Ghost Powder that had been sprinkled on the surface of the trees fell, revealing a large area of green leaves.

The movement of the hand soon attracted a few sloths. They took out the Ghost Powder from their pockets again and went to sprinkle it to the hand.

This was exactly what Pearson wanted, so he used his Sumeru Space to collect and store the Ghost Powder.

Several sloths kept sprinkling the Ghost Powder, which was all absorbed by the Sumeru Space.

Although they felt confused and wondered why the Ghost Powder couldn't fully cover the hand, they continued doing so. They took out all the Ghost Powder from their pockets and sprinkled until the last bit. After they had none left, they turned around and left.

Not long after, Pearson had collected almost all of the Ghost Powder. After that, the hand turned back into a single spider thread and drew back into Pearson's body.

Everything happened without anyone noticing.

After a long walk, they arrived at the nearest mountain.

One side of the mountain was rowed with circular caves. As Decker led Zen and the others towards it, many members of the Wooden Leaf race drilled out from the caves.

Chapter 4044 The Sacrificial Site As Zen and the others approached, the expressions of disgust and greed of the members of the Wooden Leaf race slowly faded.

Chapter 4045 The Eye The sky turned from vivid purple to deep blue as night fell on the Night View Island.

When the light dimmed, the light spots in the Abstruse Energy World looked more like stars.

There was a vine from the eye on King Ieuan's forehead, and it could see the top of the mountain when it stood on one side of the cave.

Squeak!"

"Not now."

Just as King Ieuan spoke, its bean-sized eyes suddenly widened to twice their size, as if it saw something shocking.

However, it hesitated for a moment when it passed by the white bull.

As the monster continued to move, it ate the entire black bull.

Splash! Soon enough, the monster dissipated with a loud bang and turned into thin white hairs that scattered on the ground.

"What are these crystals?" King Ieuan asked curiously.

White hairs also appeared about ten feet away from it.

It was not until then that King Ieuan remembered its mission. It grabbed the spirit beast bag and gently put the eye back into the bag. Then, it quickly turned around and returned to the cave. "Everybody, hurry up! Apply the Ghost Powder!" "The black bull is dead?" Pearson asked.

"Creak! Yes! Hurry up!" King Ieuan confirmed and applied the Ghost Powder on its body.

In turn, Zen, the Snake Goddess, and the Eternal Realm Hunters applied a layer of Ghost Powder on their bodies.

Zen wasn't sure if Treacherous Beings devoured each other, but they had quite a lot of Ghost Powder. Thus, Campbell also applied the Ghost Powder to his body.

As soon as they finished, four human-shaped monsters arrived in the cave.

They kept looking around, as if they were looking for something.

Moreover, they exuded such an intimidating aura that everyone tried their best to resist the urge to escape.

After the white-haired monsters had searched for a while, one of them suddenly turned and looked at Zen, then strode towards him.

He only frowned and did not move, but every muscle in his body tightened.

Even though he did not know how to deal with the monster, he would never wait for death.

When the monster finally approached him, it stretched out its hand, brushed past his ear, and slapped the wall.

He carefully turned his head, only to see that the monster had targeted the plant that just sprouted on the wall.

No wonder the sloth sprinkled the Ghost Powder on the trees! The whitehaired monsters also ate plants.

Then, the white-haired monsters searched every corner of the cave and made sure that there was no "living creature" left for them to devour.

Afterward, they exploded into a pile of messy white hairs and gradually disappeared.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi let out a sigh of relief. "They finally left."

"Squeak! They won't come back again," said King Ieuan.

On the other hand, the Snake Goddess frowned in thought. "They rely on the life energy to find their prey, right? After we apply the Ghost Powder, we are like dead people," she stated.

Generally speaking, the Eternal Realm warriors present had sharp senses.

Today, however, they became too nervous because of the Treacherous Being. They had not realized that fact until the Snake Goddess reminded them.

The Ghost Powder almost entirely blocked the life energy. In other words, if someone applied the Ghost Powder on their bodies and lay motionless on the ground, they would look like corpses.

"I think so," Pearson said with a nod.

The Snake Goddess thought for a while and said, "I'll try again. Please don't shake off the Ghost Powder on your bodies."

"Don't..." Before Pearson could stop her, she had already removed the Ghost Powder on the back of her hand, which revealed her white and delicate skin.

Just then, white hairs slowly began to pile up not far away from the cave.

Not long after, the white-haired monsters appeared again and rushed towards the Snake Goddess.

Yet, she remained calm. She wasn't even in a hurry to reapply the Ghost Powder. Instead, she raised her hand and retreated slowly, luring the whitehaired monsters to follow her.

'What a crazy woman!' Pearson thought helplessly.

Chapter 4046 The Glazed Crystals The Snake Goddess had figured it out! "These creatures can't see anything. They can only chase after the life energy..." As she spoke, she applied a layer of Ghost Powder on her hand.

The white-haired monster that had been chasing her immediately stopped in its tracks. Confused, it began to sniff and search around.

The Snake Goddess's eyes flashed as her mind raced. "The races on the island all know how to use the Ghost Powder, which means the whitehaired monsters should not be a threat to them. The Wooden Leaf race are willing to offer their prey to the white-haired monsters, so there must be some sort of exchange. What do they get out of this? How do they benefit?"

"It's hard to guess." Zen shook his head. "Maybe after offering their prey, they can go somewhere to receive the so-called 'benefits'."

There were too many possibilities, and it was difficult to deduce with extremely limited clues.

"Squeak! By the way, when I used the heavenly eye to observe the Grass Bulls, the white-haired monster swallowed a Grass Bull and left some transparent glazed crystals," King Ieuan suddenly reminded.

Just now, it was busy applying the Ghost Powder, so it failed to share this.

The Snake Goddess immediately looked at Pearson and asked, "Pearson, do you have any more Grass Bull in your spirit beast bag?"

"Yes." Pearson nodded, understanding immediately. Without hesitation, he took out a Grass Bull from the spirit beast bag.

Having been summoned into the world, the Grass Bull felt the strange aura from the white-haired monster. It was immediately frightened and wanted to run away.

But before it could do so, Pearson pointed at its head. With a loud thud, the Grass Bull fell to the ground, in a deep coma.

The white-haired monster was about to leave, but when it felt the life energy of the Grass Bull, it immediately turned around and pounced on it.

In a few seconds, it had devoured almost all of the Grass Bull's flesh. When it was done eating, it disintegrated into a pile of white hairs and disappeared.

Ding, ding, ding...

As the pile of white hairs disappeared, several glazed crystals fell to the ground with crisp sounds.

These crystals were thin and long, like glass needles.

The Snake Goddess stepped forward and picked up the crystals one by one.

She placed them in her hands and looked at them carefully. These crystals gave her a feeling of discomfort, as if they were a part of the Treacherous Being, and their aura was similar.

"This should be what the Wooden Leaf race is after. If we are devoured, they will get a lot more crystals," the Snake Goddess said as she handed the crystals to Fuxi.

Fuxi held the crystals close to his face and he sniffed them carefully. After studying them in his hand for a bit, he shrugged helplessly. He couldn't shed any more light on the matter. He handed them over to Eastern Emperor Taiyi, who then handed them over to Yasamin.

Each of them took turns to observe the crystals, and finally they landed with Zen. As Zen studied them carefully, Campbell beside him asked, "Can I have a look?"

Campbell had the body of the Treacherous Being, so his perception was completely different from theirs'.

Zen nodded and gave them to him. Then, Campbell clenched his fist, crystals in hand. Slowly, he closed his eyes and stood still.

Campbell's face suddenly began to melt, like wax off a candle. His human body quickly melted into a pool of white and translucent mud, and his armor was clattered all over the ground.

"Master Campbell!" Zen shouted in a hurry.

"What's wrong with him?"

"Why is this happening?"

"Are these glazed crystals used to deal with the Treacherous Beings?"

Anxiety was written all over the faces of the others.

Although Campbell was only a hostility-level Treacherous Being, he was still the builder of the world! His understanding of the entire chaos far surpassed that of the others. He was indispensable to the group.

If something went wrong because of a few unknown glazed crystals...

"Look, those glazed crystals!" King Ieuan said as it pointed at Campbell.

The previous few glazed crystals had drilled into Campbell's body and were completely wrapped up.

"Let's wait and see. Maybe the situation is not as bad as we think," the Snake Goddess said.

After all, Campbell's Treacherous Being body only melted, but it hadn't eroded. The body of the Treacherous Being was deathless after all, and as long as it could recover, it would be fine.

About fifteen minutes later, the mud formed by Campbell began to shake. A head slowly emerged out of the transparent white mud, and his body slowly returned to the human form.

"Master Campbell, what happened to you just now?" Zen asked, his forehead creasing with worry.

Campbell opened his clenched fist, and the glazed crystals were still in his hand. Eyeing them fondly, he said, "These things seem to be my home. I feel comfortable and want to sleep in them..."

As a unique creature, the Treacherous Being was naturally completely different from a normal creature.

When Campbell held these crystals, he felt sleepy, as if these crystals were a bed beckoning for him.

As soon as he turned into the mud, he took a short nap.

After Campbell returned the crystals to Zen, Zen relayed to the others what Campbell had just told him.

"Sleep..." Eastern Emperor Taiyi frowned slightly.

Sleep was something that weak creatures needed.

A soul which had been tempered would never have the need to sleep.

There was no doubt that the Treacherous Being possessed a more powerful and special soul. However, just now, Campbell had taken a nap! This confused Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

"Maybe this kind of thing can hypnotize the Treacherous Being," Thurston guessed, gesturing at the crystals.

Staring at the glazed crystals in Zen's hand, the Snake Goddess frowned deeply. "Master Campbell has woken up, but he is still unable to resist the crystals. What would happen to the Treacherous Beings which haven't woken up, if they are exposed to such crystals?"

No matter they belonged to the attaching type or the killing type, these Treacherous Beings all relied on their wills to act, without too much judgment.

Wouldn't these Treacherous Beings fall into a coma if they came into contact with these crystals? "Maybe they can be used to trap the Treacherous Beings," Pearson said.

The Snake Goddess nodded slightly, but her eyebrows still furrowed. She felt that these glazed crystals were more useful than they were letting on.

"We don't have to think too much. The mystery will solve itself at dawn,"

Sawyer suddenly said.

When the Snake Goddess heard this, her mouth twitched upwards into a smile. "You're right!"

They weren't ruthless and merciless, but the members of the Wooden Leaf race couldn't blame them for anything they did, as they even dared to trap them and sacrifice their lives.

The night of the Night View Island lasted for twenty hours.

After they applied the Ghost Powder, no other white-haired monsters broke into the cave that night.

King Ieuan once again took out the heavenly eye from the spirit beast bag and observed the situation outside.

Occasionally, it heard the screams of some creatures. When it looked into the direction where the sound rang out, it could see the white-haired monsters devouring some unfortunate sacrifices.

Twenty hours later, dawn broke, and the sky gradually lightened.

As the sun rose, so did everyone's downtrodden spirits.

In a small cave at the bottom of the mountain, Decker came out and shook off the Ghost Powder on his body.

The other members of the Wooden Leaf race also came out of their small 'houses', including their leader, Graham.

Decker and Graham locked eyes, excitement written all over their faces.

Chapter 4047 The Arcanum The Night View Island was rather peculiarly named. Whoever didn't apply the Ghost Powder on this island would die at night.

As those strangers knew nothing, they would have been eaten by the whitehaired monsters last night.

"I'm wondering how many Arcana were left," Graham thought out loud with eyes shining with greed.

Over the past few years, because of the appearance of the Evil Tiger race, the west path of the Wooden Leaf race had been cut off. As a result, hunting had become more and more difficult as time had passed. These strangers could not have come at a more fortunate time.

Graham hadn't slept a wink last night and had been hiding in his cave in fear. But now, it was time to harvest.

"They are humans," Decker said with a strong desire in his eyes. "And what's more, they are quite strong when you think about it. I think the white-haired monsters must have left a lot of Arcana!"

The two of them called the other soldiers of the Wooden Leaf race and then climbed up the stairs at the side of the mountain.

Although both Decker and Graham sincerely believed that Zen and his companions had been devoured completely, they still had to be prepared for any unexpected situations that might arise.

The Wooden Leaf race was very good with bows and arrows. The soldiers held simply wooden bows in their hands, but the arrows were cyan black and poisonous. These arrows were known to be incredibly toxic. That was the sole reason the seemingly weak members of the Wooden Leaf race had survived so long.

In the blink of an eye, they had climbed the mountainside and arrived at the cave.

Decker signaled to the crowd. They held their breath and approached quietly.

The soldiers were walking gingerly and slowly approached the side of the cave. Decker was the first to poke his head into the cave, and he was extremely careful in doing so. But there was nothing and no one in it.

Chances were, those humans had been eaten up by the white-haired monsters. Decker had already expected this outcome. He felt more relieved and then looked to the ground.

If those humans had been completely annihilated, then there would be a lot of things left behind there.

Decker's eyes swept over the ground, and his pupils suddenly shrank. He was staring at the center of the cave, where only four glazed crystals were sitting sadly.

"So few?" Decker narrowed his eyes.

"Not even half a dozen crystals?" Graham frowned.

Decker walked in and picked up the glazed crystals on the ground.

Normally, after the white-haired monsters had devoured their prey, Decker and his companions could obtain at least ten glazed crystals. If those humans really had been eaten up by the white-haired monsters, then there should be at least a hundred glazed crystals lying on the ground.

But there were only four here! Only two possibilities could explain this.

The first one was that the humans were still alive, or it could be that the glazed crystals had been stolen.

A bad feeling rose from the bottom of Decker's and Graham's hearts.

They were sincerely hoping that the second option was the right one.

If those humans were still alive, then Decker and company were in deep trouble.

As the two of them pondered over the mystery, they suddenly felt the leaves above their heads become extremely heavy. The leaves were quickly turning red.

The members of the Wooden Leaf race had a talent quite similar to what the Augury Dog had, in the sense that they could predict danger in advance.

And perhaps it was because they were good at archery, their talent was also more practical than that of the Augury Dog. They could sense the presence of their enemies from a distance. This complemented their archery skills since arrows could kill from a distance.

Unfortunately, their enemies were rather close this time.

Zen and his group were hiding in the cave, but they were covered with a layer of skin from Sawyer's treasure, known as the Magic Camouflage Skin.

It could change into any form and color.

The moment Sawyer removed the Magic Camouflage Skin, Zen reached out his hand and grabbed the bow in Decker's hand.

Decker's reaction was also incredibly fast. He raised his hand and was about to shoot an arrow at Zen.

The other warriors of the Wooden Leaf race also followed suit. Bows and arrows were their weapons of choice, and operating them was in their instinct. Therefore, their reaction speed and accuracy were both very high.

However, this time, something unfortunate happened. Before Decker or anyone else had a chance to let an arrow fly, a thin strand of spider thread was wrapped around their arrows.

And when they were about to shoot, the spider thread pulled the arrows away in one direction. The soldiers of the Wooden Leaf race could do nothing but stare at their bows in confusion.

Crack! Just two of Zen's fingers pinched Decker's bow and crushed it with a gentle force.

Crack! Crack! Crack! The bows of the other members of the Wooden Leaf race shared a similar fate.

Fuxi, the Snake Goddess, and the Eternal Realm Hunters also made their moves and crushed the long bows of whoever was nearest.

The Wooden Leaf race was quickly detained.

"You, you... What do you want?" Decker's face turned pale.

"Friends from afar, why are you doing this to us? Have we been ungracious hosts to you?" Graham asked in a calm tone.

As the patriarch of the Wooden Leaf race, he was much calmer than Decker in times of crisis.

However, his calm was immediately lost when he heard the unmistakable crack of bones breaking into two! Crack! The warrior behind Graham had tried to pull out his short sword and attack Pearson in secret, but his neck was immediately broken. His large head rolled to a side, and the sound of spurting blood could be heard coming from the cave.

Swish! Swish! Swish! Silver threads wrapped themselves around the necks of Decker and all his friends. And these were not as fragile as ordinary spider threads.

Instead, they felt as sharp as sword blades.

Pearson's cold eyes were full of killing intent now. "Stop talking nonsense.

And don't try any unnecessary flattery, or you will die immediately."

"How dare you..."

Crack! Sizzle! Sizzle! Sizzle! Another soldier of the Wooden Leaf race was about to threaten Pearson, but the latter immediately moved his finger and the sharp thread cut off the soldier's neck before he could complete his sentence.

As his detached head fell to the ground, so did a cold silence in the cave.

Not a single soldier of the Wooden Leaf race dared to say anything now.

Pearson was gazing at them fiercely, but they did not even dare to look into his eyes.

The man's intention had been to catch Decker and torture him cruelly yesterday.

Although the method that Zen and the others proposed could also achieve his goal and was more secure, it was too troublesome in his eyes.

Graham and Decker had initially planned on struggling, but now, they completely gave up.

Without further ado, Zen took out a glazed crystal and placed it in front of Decker. "What is this?" he asked.

Decker rolled his eyes, but Pearson threatened, "Answer him now, or you will die."

As soon as he finished speaking, the silver threads wrapped around Decker's and Graham's necks magically tightened themselves. The sharp threads cut into their flesh, and blood quickly seeped out.

"It's an Arcanum!"

"It's an Arcanum!"

Decker and Graham cried out simultaneously.

"Very good." Pearson waved at Zen and said, "Go on."

Zen and the others were a little confused when they heard this strange name. Zen continued the interrogation, "What's the use of this Arcanum?"

"It gets its name from the fact that the Treacherous Beings like it very much. If we accumulate enough of this, we can easily subdue them by distracting them," Decker explained.

"Is that all?" Zen asked.

Decker hesitated, but trembled when his eyes met Pearson's. He quickly replied, "No. If you refine it, you can coexist peacefully with several Treacherous Beings without having to worry about subduing them. You can also turn them into your own weapons and even a part of your body. Then you would be half human and half Treacherous Being."

Chapter 4048 The Thorny Treacherous Being "Half Treacherous Being?"

Everyone wore strange expressions of mingled shock, calculation, and curiosity.

The literal meaning of the sentence was not difficult to understand.

But the question was, which side would dominate? Would the body be ruled by the mind of the human, or the mind of the Treacherous Being? When Campbell had possessed Zen's body, Zen had been unable to resist his will at all. Campbell completely dominated the human body. Thus, everyone was inclined to think that becoming half human and half Treacherous Being was the equivalent of suicide.

"If one merges with a Treacherous Being, aren't they afraid that the Treacherous Being will suppress their consciousness and rule over them?"

the Snake Goddess asked, voicing everyone's main concern.

"Yes, that's possible," Decker admitted. He explained, "When some Treacherous Beings of the friendly type wake up, some will snatch their hosts' bodies, and others won't. However, the Treacherous Beings' power is very strong. It's worth taking a risk."

Decker's words made some sense.

Indeed, there were creatures who wouldn't hesitate to sacrifice their very lives in order to obtain greater strength and power.

The Snake Goddess nodded. She asked, "You mention a 'friendly type' of Treacherous Beings. Could you explain what you mean by that?"

"They are kindhearted Treacherous Beings, harmless to others," Decker replied. "These good Treacherous Beings are willing to help others, and this is their will. For example, the Treacherous Beings in the form of sloths in the forest are among the friendly-type ones."

The sloths were tireless in applying the Ghost Powder on the surface of the trees, to prevent the trees from being devoured by the white-haired monsters.

Moreover, after they saw Zen and the others in his group, they had also brought out the Ghost Powder to remind them to apply it.

But Zen and his companions were still wary of the sloths, and found it difficult to trust them completely.

Pearson's eyes were blank. His face was expressionless as he lifted one hand, gently holding up the length of silver thread. The other end of the thread was tightly wrapped around the necks of Decker and Graham.

Pearson wanted to kill one of them, so that the remaining one wouldn't dare to lie to them.

Decker was smart enough to see what Pearson intended, so he didn't dare to hide anything from them. He told them everything he knew, but Pearson clearly still had doubts. "The white-haired monsters will also devour those plants. You can directly cut the trees and pick the flowers in exchange for the 'Arcana'," Pearson said flatly. A cold light flashed in his emotionless eyes. "Why did you deceive us into coming here?"

"The white-haired monsters will indeed devour plants, but devouring plants won't produce 'Arcanum'," answered Decker quickly.

Pearson shrugged. Fuxi stepped forward and asked, "Have any of you merged with a Treacherous Being and become half human and half Treacherous Being?"

Since entering the Supreme Pure Realm, Fuxi had felt that his strength was completely insufficient.

Although he had the Light of Annihilation, it was not enough. In fact, for most of his time in these two realms, he'd ended up running for his life.

Naturally, the idea of becoming half human and half Treacherous Being intrigued him, as it presented the possibility of obtaining more power.

"The warriors of our Wooden Leaf race all are half human and half Treacherous Being," answered Decker.

"Really?" Fuxi said, sounding surprised. His eyes widened, for he had expected a more conservative answer.

Zen and the others also looked surprised.

They had assumed that, at most, one or two members of the Wooden Leaf race had successfully merged with a Treacherous Being and become half human and half Treacherous Being.

But now Decker was telling them that all the warriors of the Wooden Leaf race were half human and half Treacherous Being, which was an incredible number.

Pearson's eyes narrowed and he tightened his grip on the silver spider thread with increased vigilance. The thread tightened on Graham's and Decker's necks, and the blood which had already begun to dry now flowed out once more.

"Don't—don't be nervous," Decker gasped, feeling blood dripping down his neck from the tight grip of the thread.

Graham swiftly added, "There are variations in the levels of strength possessed by Treacherous Beings. Our Wooden Leaf race is relatively weak, so the Treacherous Beings we merged with are not that strong."

Pearson's grip loosened slightly. "You're right," he said. "Otherwise, you wouldn't have fallen into this situation."

"Then prove your words," Zen ordered. He was not worried that this command would cause any problems for him and his group.

After all, Zen had already managed to kill the three stone men who were also half human and half Treacherous Being.

The skills of the Wooden Leaf race were centered on archery, not direct combat. They were not much stronger than the stone men, since the space here was limited, and they could not bring their strength into full play.

Under Zen's instruction, Pearson loosened the silver spider thread even further. The leader of the race, Graham, felt much better. He lifted his hand to touch the thread still wrapped around his neck.

With the silver thread tied around him, Graham walked several steps, towards the center of the cave. He took out a small glass bottle from within the folds of his clothing. This glass bottle was made of "Arcana", and it contained a small thorny ball, which was a Treacherous Being.

"Can I use arrows?" asked Graham.

Zen nodded. He gazed at the thorny ball within the glass bottle and said, "But doesn't the Arcanum need to be refined within one's body?"

"The Treacherous Beings that haven't woken up are not suitable to stay inside one's body for a long time," Graham explained. "Otherwise they will affect the warrior's body and mind."

Most Treacherous Beings released an aura that would make other creatures very uncomfortable. Even the sloths, which were supposedly the friendly type of Treacherous Beings, had such an aura. Only the Treacherous Beings that had woken up would not make people feel disgusted.

Graham lightly knocked on the glass bottle, and the shrunken thing in the bottle began to expand and flow out. The Treacherous Being resembled a sea urchin in shape.

Everyone watched silently, and the only sound came from the movement of the Treacherous Being.

The fluid-looking sea urchin stretched and flowed into Graham's eyes, ears, mouth and nose. It seeped like liquid into the orifices, until it was all gone.

Then Graham blinked and took out a bow and arrow. His old bow had been crushed so this was a different weapon.

Although this was only intended to be a demonstration, everyone stared at Graham with alertness.

After all, he was going to display the power of the Treacherous Being.

He raised the bow and fitted the long arrow into the string. A white light gathered in his right hand as the aura of the Treacherous Being concentrated in that spot. Graham aimed his arrow at the wall of the cave and said, "The Treacherous Being I merged with is very suitable for archery. When I shoot it out, it will cause a strong destructive force."

With that, he released the bowstring in his hand.

The arrow shot forward.

As the arrow flew, the white light soared forward, converging into the point of the arrowhead.

With a crack, the arrow hit the wall of the cave.

It created a small hole as it entered the wall and burrowed inside the stone.

Zen and the others watched calmly.

It was true that the mountain walls in the Jade Pure Realm should be very difficult to destroy, but they themselves could achieve the same thing with a bow and arrow. It required the use of focused strength, and they thought that given a similar weapon, they could probably do more damage than Graham had done.

However, in the next instant, a crack spread out from the tiny hole, and began to spread out along the surface of the cave wall.

Everyone became more vigilant as the walls began to rumble.

It sounded as though something was moving within the depths of the mountain.

Graham was very familiar with the power of the thorny Treacherous Being.

He took a few steps back as the wall in front of him started to collapse. As the wall crashed, a large hole was revealed, and within it was the Treacherous Being in the shape of sea urchin.

It had grown much larger. Its body had expanded at least a hundred times in size. Colorful thorns were embedded in the rock wall around the enormous sea urchin.

This level of damage had been caused by shooting the Treacherous Being into the wall. If it had been shot into the body of a living being, they could only imagine the power of the resulting explosion.

Zen looked sharply at Graham. "All the Treacherous Beings you merged with are of this same type?" he asked.

Graham nodded. "This kind of Treacherous Beings is our first choice. After we get enough 'Arcana', we each find such a Treacherous Being to merge with."

When Pearson heard Graham's answer, his mouth twitched slightly. The fighting capacity of the Wooden Leaf race was not as bad as he had imagined.

If they had fought with the Wooden Leaf race yesterday, they might win, but there might be some casualties. It seemed that Zen and the Snake Goddess's plan was the best plan.

Meanwhile, Fuxi, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and several others were more interested in merging with Treacherous Beings.

After cultivating to the Eternal Realm, one's bloodline power couldn't change any more, and it became more difficult to find a stronger Other Shore Token. It looked like merging with Treacherous Beings was a shortcut to increase the level of one's strength.

Chapter 4049 A Trace Of Humans Fuxi, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and the others raised several more questions.

Once these questions were answered, they had a basic understanding of what the Night View Island was all about.

A large number of different races — close to a thousand — lived in the annular mountain range around the Night View Island.

It was weird but astonishing that so many races coexisted on such a small island.

One or two races were present on almost every mountain here. These races were mainly divided into three tiers and the Wooden Leaf race was among the weakest ones.

The Wooden Leaf race knew their limitations and rarely came into conflict with other races. That was how they had survived in such a complicated environment.

"Did you capture your Treacherous Beings in the mountains?" Fuxi asked.

The Snake Goddess and the others were concerned at Fuxi's question, given that it was an important one. Why were there so many Treacherous Beings on the Night View Island? They had encountered a lot of sloth-shaped Treacherous Beings on their way to this mountain, which, according to Decker, was just the tip of the iceberg. The abundance of Treacherous Beings on the Night View Island was way beyond their imagination.

Decker shook his head and said, "Most Treacherous Beings in the mountains are weak and the powerful ones are mainly the killing type. The killing type also likes Arcana and will kill you to plunder your Arcana.
